svīyasadasyān nirāpaddūratve sthāpayati sma 
bhāṣā sāhitya
sāmājikī prathā dharmaḥ ca svātantryena viracitāḥ 
  manuṣyasya ca tasya saskṛteḥ madhye yatnakṛtasambandhaviṣayakaḥ bauddhaprekṣāpaṭaḥ pāścātye śāstre śaktiśālittvānusandhānāya avadāna racayati 
yatra adhunā mānasikavikṛtijātakāyikaviśṛkhalāyā ālocanā paryavekṣaṇasya paryāye'vatiṣṭhate 
 asmābhistādṛśī sambhāvanā vivecanīyā yat gabhīrataramānasikarogakāraṇānā mūla tatraiva sthātumarhati yatra bauddhāḥ astāyini parivartanaśīle  
jagati durdāntā tathā asusthāmāsakti paśyanti  
mānavavyaktitasya gabhīrataramātrāyā sthāyitvāpekṣayā sāmājika parivartanamadhikatara svāsthyakara bhavitumarhati 
mānavo yadā yathārtha jīvati tadā sa sacetanaḥ komalaśca 
kintu maraṇakāle sa kaṭhoraḥ anamanīyaśca 
ata eva anamanīyatva hi mṛtyulakṣaṇam
sacetanā ca jīvanasya lakṣaṇam 
cārlasmarismahāśayaḥ tarkayati yat mokṣasya rūpa vilopasya rūpam  adhikārasūcakatāyāḥ kasyacit rūpasya vilopaḥ 
jīvanasya sārabhūta vastu anamanīyeṣu viścaleṣu rūpeṣu na dṛśyate
kintu pratiṣṭhitaniyamasya viphalīkaraṇeṣu 
sthāyistirasāmājikaniyamāya manuṣyasya ākāṅkṣā vartate 
atiśayena tadākāṅkṣā varṇanāyā sārvalaukika prāvaṇyamida tathya varṇayati yat tathā mārkasamahodaya āha
manuṣyaḥ tattvād vahiḥ avasthite jagati vasati 
eṣā sambhāvanā yāvanna gauraveṇa gṛhyate
 tāvat asmāka prativeśijīvānā samṛddhaye mūlyavān mānasikasvāsthyakāryakramaḥ tathā parahitaiṣivyāpāraḥ pariṇāme kevalamanyat yantra bhavitumarhati 
yat yantramatyāvaśyakasāmājikapraṇodanā dṛḍhīkaroti 
tatraiva sarvavidhānā mānasikānā tathā āvegaprasūtānā viśṛkhalānā mūla varttate 
abauddhodyameṣu ekam antima vaiśiṣṭyamullekhayogyam
yena samājasthamanuṣyasambandhīyabodho jāyate 
eṣu bavavaḥ sāmājikāvasthāyāḥ eka vaiśiṣṭya nirdiśanti 
tathā hi ārthanītikaśaktayaḥ
pratiṣṭhitā dharmāḥ
ādarśāḥ rājanītisamparkitā vyavasthā
acividyāsakrāntā vyavasthā ca 
ete khalu vyavahārasya pradhānā nirdhārakāḥ 
vyaktitvasampariktasāskṛtapaścātpaṭādhyayana kadāpi vā sāmājikacaritrākāreṇa mukhyaprabhāvatvena śiśuśālā samīkṣyate 
bauddhamānasikatāyā eko guṇo hi eva yat eṣā mānasikatā ekasmin upādāne pradhāna nirdhāraka paśyati
yat samādheyasamasyāyām svaya na prayujyate 
idamucyate yat mānavavyavahāraḥ mūlataḥ kenacit sāmājikena upādānena  yathā ārthanītika jīvanam nirdhāryate 
uttarākāreṇa vartamānamapi praśnāśatveneda vyavahriyate iti pratibhāti
yadi pāścātye sarvajanaḥ vaśānukrameṇa ida na karoti
aya nirṇayaḥ sukhataro bhaviṣyati kathametāḥ sarvā mānasikatāḥ praśna prārthayante 
manuṣyaḥ pṛthivyāḥ vividhāsu saskṛtiṣu kārya karoti 
 sa kathamittham ācarati ityasya uttaratvena yadeva ekaikam upādāna gṛhyate tadeva svaya prahelikāvastu yasya samādhānam anveṣaṇaparameva 
bauddhapaścāt paṭa ima praśna na prārthayate 
tathāpi bauddhaviśleṣanasya pradhāno guṇo hi eva yat ida samāje manuṣya sambandhiprakṛtapraśnasabodhanāya samartham 
katha tasya abhyāsāḥ santi  aya na praśnaḥ 
kintu katha sa teṣā parivartanāya na svīkaroti iti praśnaḥ
yadyapi ida sarveṣu spaṣṭa yat vartamānajīvanaśailyām yā calamānatāsti sā tasya samagrā sabhyatāmucchetturmarhati 
asya praśnasya uttara
buddhaḥ tarkayati
bādhyatāmūlake samparke vartate 
pratyeka mānavaḥ tatsamparka saskṛtau dhārayati yatra sa vasati 
caturtho'dhyāyaḥ bauddhadharme premakaruṇayoḥ prakṛtiḥ sarve sukhino bhavantu pā yaḥ 
 iti hṛdayānubhūtericchayā prakāśita sārabhūta vastu eva prema pada saśliṣṭopadeśāntareṇāpi viśeṣaṇa pada saśliṣṭopadeśāntareṇāpi viśeṣaṇapremipadasamparkitopadeśā  
api savādeṣu vartante  
prativiṣaya pṛthag gurutvamasti iti kārāṇāt pratyeka viṣayavastu aparasmādeva yatheṣṭa pṛthak 
ekasya viṣayamadhikṛtya yā uktayaḥ santi tāḥ sādhāraṇataḥ anyasya kṣetre na prayojyāḥ 
aṅgulichoṭikāviṣayakakṣudratarasavāde gotamaḥ sannyāsino vadati yat
yo janoaṅgulichoṭikākālamapi karuṇāmaya citta poṣayati sa jano bhikṣuriti ucyate 
aṅguttaranikāya 
buddhaḥ punarapi vadapi  yo jano'ṅgulichoṭikākāla karuṇāmaya citta karṣati bhāveti
 athavā tat citta prati manoyoga karoti
so'pi yathārtha bhikṣuḥ 
gotamo vyākhyāti 
yat īdṛśasya bhikṣoḥ dhyānamagnatā vṛthā na gacchati 
yataḥ sa upadeśānanusṛtya karma karoti 
tathā ca yathāyatha rājya bhuṅkte bhuñjati 
attaranikāya  
kṣudratarachoṭikā sthānasya ṭīkā vyākhyāti yat aya savādaḥ agnijvālayā saha tulanāmadhikṛtya yaḥ savādaḥ tasya antimāśaḥ 
agnijvālāsavāde gotamaḥ sannyāsina upadiśati yat agnijvālāsahanam api vara
ki vā paraduḥkhasahana varam
tathāpi strīsaṅgo na kāmanīyaḥ
paradravyabhogaḥ na kartavyaḥ vā parasraparidhāna vā na kartavyam paribhujñjeyya
aguttaranikāya  
 agninā dagdhaḥ san bhikṣuḥ kañcit kāla kaṣṭa prāpsyati
athavā kaṣṭatamāvasthāyā mariṣyati 
kintu sa yadi strīsage tiṣṭhati athavā strīkhādya gṛhṇāti
strīvastrādīnā paridhāna karoti
tarhi punareva narake janma grahīṣyati
tatra ca sa cira duḥkha prāpsyati 
evañca anyavidhaspaṣṭadṛṣṭantaiḥ gotamaḥ siddhānta jñāpayati  kena prakāreṇa bhikṣavo'nuśīlana kuryuḥ
arthāt yadi te buddhasya upadeśamanusaranti tarhi teṣā bhikṣāyāstathā paridheyasya vastunaḥ prayogo yathāyatha bhaviṣyati 
sa āha  bho bhikṣavaḥ
yuṣmābhiḥ nimnavidhopāyenābhyāsaḥ kartavyaḥ 
vaya pīḍitāḥ santaḥ bhikṣābhojya vastramāśrayamauṣadha ca bhuñjmahe 
tāni dravyāṇi ye dātāro dadati te mahat phala tathā hita labhante 
asmāka tyāgadharmaḥ puraskāra prāpsyati 
aya saphalo bhaviṣyati
aya vṛthā na yāsyati 
bhikṣavaḥ yuṣmābhiḥ uparyuktenopāyenābhyāsaḥ karttavyaḥ 
bhikṣavaḥ yūya yadi hita paśyatha
tarhi yūya yatnena ceṣṭadhvam 
yūya yadi parahita paśyatha
tarhi yūya yatnena ceṣṭadhvam 
yadi yūyamubhayahita paśyatha
tarhi yatnena yūya ceṣṭadhvam 
aguttaranikāya 
asminnanucchede ida spaṣṭa yat bhikṣoḥ prayojanīyadravyāṇā bhogamadhikṛtya prāgvartinī uktiḥ anucitopāya nirdiśati 
aya na bhogo'nucitatvāt 
indriyatṛptyartha yo bhogaḥ
tasmāt bhikṣuḥ narake janma labhate 
varam tena dātṛhitakāraka karma karaṇīyam
dharmīyajīvanopayogihitasādhaka karma sampādanīyam 
agnijvālāsavādaḥ etāvān prabhāvavānāsīt yat yasya prabhāvāt ṣaṣṭiḥ bhikṣavaḥ raktavamana kṛtavantaḥ
ṣaṣṭiḥ bhikṣavaḥ sannyāsa tyaktavantaḥ
apare ṣaṣtiḥ bhikṣavaḥ sampūrṇa muktā abhavan 
aguttaranikāya 
kṣudratarachoṭikāviṣayikī ṭīkā varṇayati yat agnijvālānuśāsanāt para buddhaḥ pakṣakāla nibhṛtavāsa cakāra 
yadā sa vahirāgataḥ tadā sa svalpasasthakān janānapaśyat 
aguttaranikāyaṭīkā manorathapūraṇī  
tadīyo'nujaḥ sahacaraśca ānandaḥ āha yat bahubhiḥ bhikṣubhiḥ sannyāsastyaktaḥ yataste'nubhavanti yat te dharmīyajīvanayāpane'samarthāḥ
te'nubhavanti yat
yadi te'nucitamācaranti tarhi viśvastaiḥ dātṛbhiḥ pradattānā dravyānā bhogaḥ anucito bhaviṣyati 
buddho vismitaḥ sannāha tasya nibhṛtavāsakāle na kenāpi bhikṣūṇā samīpe sukhaśvāsakāraṇam assāsakāraṇa
vyākhyātam 
tadabhyāsena bhikṣavo niścayena jñāsyanti yat te dattadravyāṇā vyavahāra yathāyatha kurvanti 
kṣudratarachoṭikākāṭīkāyā buddha ānandamavadat yat samudragāmino yathā bahavo mārgāḥ tiṣṭhanti
tathā tadīye upadeśe sukhaśvāsakāraṇāni vahūnyeva santi 
aguttaranikāya ṭīkā
manorathapūraṇī  
sa sannyāsināmāhvānāya ānandamādideśa 
tataḥ eka mukhabandha dadau  bho bhikṣavaḥ
premṇaḥ prāthamikaḥ paryāya eva eka sukhaśvāsakāraṇam mettaya sabbapubbabhaga 
atra kevala jīvahitasādhanāya jīvaiḥ saha sambandhastiṣṭhati 
eṣā na yathārthataḥ karuṇā 
aguttaranikāyaṭīkā 
punaśca ṭīkāyāmuyate yat ālocanābinduvyākhyānāya buddhaḥ agulichoṭikāviṣayakakṣudratarākhyānasya avatāraṇā cakāra 
aguttaranikāyaṭīkā  
  eva agnijvālāyāḥ upasahāratvena kṣudratarachoṭikāsavādaḥ ta mārga nirdiśati yatra karuṇāyāḥ prāthamikaḥ paryāyaḥ hi sukhaśvāsakāraṇamiti  
vyākhyātam  
idamullekhya yat  yathā ṭīkāyā dṛśyate  buddhaḥ karuṇāmayacittasya paryāyatraya pratiṣṭhāpayati 
tathā hi   prāthamikaḥ paryāyaḥ  yatra kevala jīvahitecchā tiṣṭhati 
 karuṇāpraveśamukhamyatraikāgratā janma labhate 
tataśca  ekāgratāsthāpanā  yatra samādhiḥ sthāna labhate 
sādhāraṇataḥ yaugikaḥ karuṇāmayacittaśabdaḥ uktārthatrayāṇāmanyatamārtha prakāśayati 
kṣudratarachoṭikāsavāde prāthamiko'rthaḥ prakāśitaḥ 
 kṣudratarachoṭikākhyāne gotame vyākhyāti yadi koapi bhikṣuḥ agulichoṭikākālamapi karuṇāmaya citta poṣati tarhi sa yathārthato bhikṣuriti  
ucyate  
karuṇāmaya citta sacetanajīvaiḥ saha samparka sthāpayati  yatra maṅgalecchā vartate 
aguttaranikāya ṭīkā 
asya sārvalaukikaḥ paridhirasti sarve jīvāḥ sukhino bhavantu  īdṛśī icchāsmin citte jāyate 
kena prakāreṇa bhikṣuḥ īdṛśa citta poṣati tasya viśleṣaṇa ṭīkāyāmasti 
tathā hi  poṣati 
sa katha poṣati 
yadā sa cintayati tadā sa ida poṣati 
yadā jānāti
tadā sa ida poṣati 
yadā sa paśyati
tadā ida citta sa pālayati 
sapratyaya siddhāntakāle sa ida pālayati 
śaktiprayogakāle sa ida dhārayati 
jñānenopalabdhau sa ida poṣayati 
yadā sa pratyakṣajñānena jñātaya viṣaya jānāti tadā sa karuṇāmaya citta dhārayati 
tyaktavyaviṣayatyāgakāle ida sa poṣayati 
cintanīyaviṣayacintanasamaye sa ida poṣayati 
tattvataḥ pratyakṣīkaraṇīyaviṣayapratyakṣīkaraṇakāle'pi sa ida poṣayati 
kiñca cittapoṣaṇavyāpāro'ya kevala kalyāṇakāmanayā sacetanajīvasamparkitānuraktibhāvena upalabdho bhavet 
ayameva premṇaḥ prāthamikaḥ paryāyaḥ 
eva bhikṣuḥ sarvadā dharmīyakarmaṇi karuṇāmaya manaḥ pālayatimarhati 
sa yadi kevalamaṅgalichoṭikākālamapi premṇastathā karuṇāyāḥ prāthamike paryāye citta pālayati tarhi sa bhikṣuriti parigaṇyate 
tathākaraṇena sa upadeśānusāreṇa karma karoti
dhyānābhyāsa karoti tathā rājyasya bhojya bhuṅkte yathāyatham 
aguttaranikāya 
sa sukhena śvāsa grahītumalam 
kṣudratarachoṭikāyāḥ ṭīkā ta pāṭhamupanayati yatredamivocyate yat neda bhuñjati
 kintu paribhuñjati aguttaranikāyaṭīkā 
agnijvālāyā' 'paribhuñjati' ityeka pradhāna padam 
'kṣudrachoṭikātaḥ asya padasya sayojanena dvayoḥ savādayoḥ madhye samparke gurutvamāropitam 
ṭīkāyāmucyate yat agulichoṭikākālamapi karuṇāmaya citta pālayan bhikṣuḥ kena prakāreṇa rājyasya khādyadravyamapacayaśūnya bhuṅkte' 
paribhuñjati
sa 'paribhuñjati' 
paribhogaḥ caturvidhāḥ 
steyaparibhogaḥ
ṛṇaparibhogaḥ
rikthaparibhogaḥ
prabhutvena paribhogaśceti 
asmin viṣaye
duṣṭācaraṇayukto bhikṣuryadā dāna bhuṅkte
tadā steyaparibhoga ucyate 
yadā sadācārayukto bhikṣuḥ niścinta ṛṇakṛta dāna bhuṅkte
tadā ṛṇaparibhoga ucyate 
yadā śikṣārthinā sapta saghāḥ dāna bhuñjate
tadā rikthaparibhogo bhavati 
yadi bhikṣuḥ hānikara prabhāva vinaśya dāna bhuṅkte
tadā prabhutvena paribhoga ucyate 
asmin viṣaye
bhikṣuḥ kṣudratarachoṭikāyā varṇitaḥ
apacayaśūnya rājyasya bhojya bhuṅkte 
tatra kāraṇadvayamasti
prathamataḥ
yo bhikṣuḥ kevala agulichoṭikākāla karuṇā poṣayati
sa prabhutvena
ṛṇamuktatvena
rikthabhāgitvena rājyasya bhojya bhuṅkte 
idameva kāraṇa yat so'pacaya vinā rājyasya khādya bhuṅkte 
dvitīyataḥ
agulichoṭikākālamapi kāruṇikāya bhikṣave dānasya mahatī śaktirasti 
īdṛśāya bhikṣave yo dātā upahāra yacchati sa tasmādupahārāt mahat phalam
mahat hitam
mahat gaurava ca labhate 
idameva dvitīya kāraṇa yasmāt bhikṣuḥ apacaya na kṛtvā rājyasya bhojya bhuṅkte 
aguttaranikāya ṭīkā
 tulanā  visuddhimagga
yo bhikṣuḥ kṣaṇamapi prāthamikaparyāyabhuktapremakaruṇāyukta hṛdaya pālayati sa ta dharmamarjayati yo dharmastādṛśena bhikṣuṇā arjyate sa
yaḥ dānaprakṛti cintayati
yaḥ saptaśikṣārthināmanyatamaḥ bhavati
yena vā hānikarāḥ sarve prabhāvā vinaṣṭāḥ 
sa eva eko'rhaḥ 
saptavargīyāḥ śikṣārthinaḥ panthāna pratyakṣīkurvanti
athavā srotaḥpraveśinaḥ
sakṛdāgāminaḥ
anāgāminaḥ
arhataśca phalamabhijānanti 
 premamayacittānuśīlanakāribhikṣusasparśa yaḥ poṣaka āyāti sa tadbhikṣoḥ yānācārādibhiḥ anuprāṇito bhavati 
ida hitāvahamanupreraṇa bhaviṣyati ānandadāyakāya puraskārāya mūlam 
pṛṣṭha  ṭīkā 
ida poṣakeṇa paravartidharmasyācaraṇāya bījatvena sevitumapi alam 
kāruṇikacittapālakaḥ abhyāsakārī dharmīyajīvanasyotkṛṣṭaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ 
sa eva yathārtha nirapacaya bhikṣā bhuṅkte 
nimagnatāparyāyabhuktapremayuktacittameva viśeṣeṇa 'kāruṇikacitta'padena gamyate 
tathā hi  kramikavacaneṣu
buddhaḥ phalaprasūdharmācaraṇakāriṣu pradhāna gṛhasthamanāthapiṇḍakamupadiśati  aguttaranikāya 
bahubhyo janebhyo bhikṣāyā dānam
samagdṛṣṭimato janasya poṣāṇam srotaḥpraveśī
aguttaranikāya ṭīkā 
 api ca tat poṣaṇa bhaviṣyati sakṛdāgāmibhikṣave
anāgāmibhikṣave
arhadbhikṣave
jñānonmukhāya buddhāya
samyag jñānine
buddhapradhānāya bhikṣusaghāya
bauddhāśramanirmāṇam
buddhe dharme saghe ca āśrayagrahaṇam
ācāryapañcakaparyavekṣaṇam
kṣaṇakāla kāruṇikacittakarṣaṇam
anityatāpratyakṣīkaraṇam 
pradhānakāryāvalī kāruṇikacittacarcāyā āpekṣikatva gurutva pradarśayati 
kintu eṣā carcā muktyunmukhāntardṛṣṭicarcāyā nimne eva vartate 
kāruṇikacittamiti samastapadasya vyākhyāyā ṭīkāha  'hitasādhaneccasametasacetajīvasamparkita cittameva kāruṇika cittam 
punaśca ida yathārthataḥ samādhiyogena antarbhukto bhavati 
' aguttaranikāya ṭīkā  
evamatra kāruṇikacittam samādhiparyāyabhukta sarvathāpi premakaruṇānvita tiṣṭhati 
'krakacadṛṣṭāntasavāde' gotamaḥ bhikṣu moliyaphaggunamupadiśati yat sa kupitacittapoṣaṇa na kṛtvā kāruṇika citta pālayet 
majjhimanikāya 
moliyaphaggunaḥ sannyāsinībhiḥ saha atyanta sasaktaḥ savṛttaḥ 
tasmāt ko'pi yadi sannyāsinīnā doṣamullikhati
tarhi so'tīva kruddho jātaḥ 
evañca sannyāsinīnā pratikiyāsīt
yadi ko'pi tasyācaraṇe doṣa paśyati 
tacchrutvā buddhaḥ moliyamāhvayati sma 
sa tamāha yat sannyāsinīṣu atyāsaktiḥ sannyāsinā pakṣe anucittā 
ata eva yadi ko'pi janaḥ sannyāsinīnā vyavahāreṣu doṣa paśyati
tadā sa īdṛśa manobhāva poṣayet  mama citta viṣayagāmi na bhavatu 
aha kuvākya na vadiṣyāmi 
aha sarvebhyo hitāya sahānubhūti poṣayiṣyāmi 
mama citta kāruṇika sat sarvadā kopamukta bhaviṣyati iti 
majjhimanikāya 
buddho moliyamupadiśati yat sa samamanobhāva poṣayet yadi ko'pi tadīya doṣa paśyati
athavā ko'pi ta vā sannyāsinīḥ vā āhanti 
gotamo bhikṣūnupadiśati  na kevala parakṛtaguṇadoṣavivecanamukhe
api tu parasambandhiguṇadoṣavivecanakāle sarvadā kāruṇika citta lālayet 
savādeṣu buddho gotamo vyākhyāti yat yadi ko'pi aparasya doṣa saśodhayitumicchati
tarhi sa yathākālamida kuryāt 
tadā sa kāruṇikena hṛdayena satya vadet
śānta vadet
lābhajanakatayā kārya kuryāt 
dīghanikāya 
katha vā parasparam salapet iti upadiśya punaśca sa sayojayāmāsa yat sarve bhikṣavaḥ sarvadā sarvaiḥ saha śānta vyavahareyuḥ 
madhyamamānavacaneṣu gotama upadiśati yat ko'pi janaḥ jātivicāra na kṛtvā premamaya hṛdaya karṣet 
majjhimanikāya 
ayamabhyāso na kevala sarveṣā karttavyo'pi tu ādhyātmikamārgaparisamāptaye upayogitā vrajati 
'kassapa prati sihagarjana'  savāde gotamo varṇayati yo bhikṣuḥ kāruṇika citta pālayati
sarvān kṣatikarān prabhāvān vinaśyati āsava
 sa yathāyogya 'parivrājakaḥ' samaṇa
ucyate athavā 'brāhmaṇa' ucyate 
dīghanikāya 
atra gotamo dharmīyamādarśa varṇayati
tenādarśena vyaktipakṣe prayojanamasti yadi vyaktiḥ parivrājako vā brāhmaṇo vā bhavitumicchati 
majjhimanikāyaṭīkā
papañcasudanī 
vaktṛtāmālāyā kṣātikarāṇā viṣayāṇā sūcī āsava asti 
tatra kṣatikarā viṣayā nāma ākāṅkṣā
punarjanma
avidyā
dṛṣṭābhimatam ca 
te viṣayāḥ ṭīkāsu eva vyākhyātāḥ 
tathā hi  indriyatṛṣṇā
punarjanmākāṅkṣā
ajñatā
bhrāntamata ca 
visuddhimagga 
te viṣayāḥ kevalam arhadbhiḥ sampūrṇa parityaktāḥ 
pārthivapariveśasya prakṛtiḥ anityā 
sā prakṛtiḥ arhatā tṛpti na vidadhāti 
te sūkṣmabhāvena prakṛti yathākrama paśyanti 
tathā ca te nirvāṇasya svādamanubhavanti 
phalataḥ te na punaḥ pārthivendriyasukhenākṛṣṭā bhavanti 
evamanityasukha vā punarjanmano duḥkha vā tān prabhāvitān karttu na śaknoti 
īdṛśaiḥ janaiḥ sarvavidha mānasika tamastathā bhrānta mata dūrīkṛtam 
tataḥ arhatpadasya samaparyāyaśabdaḥ khalu 'khinasavaḥ' arthāt 'yena kṣatikaraprabhāvo vinaṣṭa' iti 
punaśca yadi īdṛśo janaḥ premamaya hṛdaya karṣati
tarhi sa yathārthataḥ parivrājakaḥ brāhmaṇo vā bhavitumarhati 
kramikavacaneṣu buddha āha bhikṣūn prati sukarmasādhanāt bhītiḥ na karaṇīyā
yataḥ sukarmapada prakṛtyā sukhaparyāyam 
aguttaranikāya 
sa svakīya jñānamullikhati yat tena cira yat sukarma kṛta tat ānandāya sampadyate 
tasyaphala caivam  sa prāktane janmani saptaparṣaiḥ kāruṇika citta pālayāmāsa 
tasmāt sa ānandamayasukhasamūha bhuṅkte 
sārvalaukike prakāśe ca vikāśe ca sapta yugāni vyāpya so'syā pṛthivyā na punarjātaḥ 
sārvalaukikaprakāśakāle sa divye jagati janmagrahaṇa cakāra ābhassara
 punaśca vikāśakāle sa divyabrāhmaprāsāde punarjanmagrahaṇamakarot 
yatra sa mahābrahmarūpeṇa rājatva cakāra 
sa āsīt 'sakkaḥ'
ākāṅkṣājagataḥ prabhuḥ
ṣaṭtriśatkṛttvaḥ
sa bahuvāra sārvalaukikaḥ samrāṭ san yathādharma śāsana cakāra 
tadā sa kāruṇika citta karṣati sma
yena sa suphala prāpnoti sma 
tasya premamaya citta samādhimārgasthaprāthamikaparyāyabhuktamāsīt 
anyasmin savāde bodhisattvasya kāruṇika tathā premamaya cittamullekhārhatā vrajati 
bhayātañkaviṣayake savāde āraṇyajīvane
sṛṣṭa sakaṭamadhikṛtya vipraḥ jāṇussoṇiḥ gotama pṛcchati
majjhimanikāya   
buddhaḥ jāṇussoṇi nivedayati yat vanavāsinā teṣā parivrājakānā brāhmaṇānā citta krodhānvita mālinyayukta cāsīt 
tasmātte bhayenātakena ca ākrāntā bhavanti 
majjhimanikāya 
sa jāṇussoṇi vyākhyāti yat ekadā sa svaya bodhisattva āsīt 
tadā buddhatvaśikṣaṇakāle so'raṇye'vasat
kintu tasya hṛdaye krodhaḥ nāsīt
tat hṛdaya premamayamāsīt 
kāruṇika citta pratyakṣīkṛtya bodhisattvaḥ kadāpi dvidhāgrastaḥ na babhūva
na vā bhītaḥ na vā ātaṅkitaḥ 
ṭīkāyāḥ sayojanamevam  mama citta krodhapūrṇa nāsīt asyāyamāśayahḥ 'mamaika karuṇāmaya hṛdayamāsīt tasmin hṛdaye hitecchā āsīt 
' bodhisattvaḥ tādṛśaḥ āsīt 
majjhimanikāyaṭīkā
papañcasudanī 
tataḥ para gotamo'smin savāde tasya samyag jñāna varṇayati
idamanumāna yukta bhavet yat araṇye bodhisattvasya jīanamadhikṛttya eṣālocanā gotamakartṛkabodhilābhāt pūrvameva yaḥ kālasta nirdiśati 
katipayeṣu savādeṣu śiṣyāḥ premamayakāyikavācikamānasikakarmaṇāmanuśīlana kurvantīti dṛśyate 
athavā te tathā karttumapadiśyante iti dṛśyate 
kaścit śiṣya eteṣāmunnataye anuprāṇito'bhavat 
yataḥ tasyāsti kāruṇika cittam dīghanikāyaṭīkā  
yathā pūrva pradarśitam
tat citta prāthamikaparyāyabhuktapremayuktamathavā samādhiparyāyabhuktapremayukta bhavitumarhati 
ṭīkāyā mate ubhayavidha citta premamayakarmasampādanāya samartha tiṣṭhati 
etā ālocanāḥ sahānubhavānupreratakāryāṇāmupari ālokasampāta kurvanti
yatra sahānubhave prāthamikaparyāyagatapremakaruṇālakṣaṇa parisphuṭam 
bhavacakrāt mahāparimuktimadhikṛtya savāde dṛśyate yat guroḥ gotamād vicchedamāsannam dṛṣṭvā ānandaḥ roditumārebhe 
dīghanikāya 
tadā gotama ānanda smārayati yat tasyaiva upadeśa evam  sarvāṇi sukhakarāṇi vastūni parivartante tirobhavanti ca 
buddhaḥ ānanda sāntvayati tadīyapremamayasevā praśasya  ānanda
tayā cireṇa sadaikyavataḥ sevā kriyate  premayakāyikakarmabhiḥ
premamayavācikakarmabhiḥ
premamayamānasikakarmabhiśca 
tāni karmāṇi hitakarāṇi
sukhāvahāni
advaitāni
parimāṇaśūnyāni ca 
dīghanikāya  
ṭīkayā viśleṣaṇamevam  premamayakāyikakarmabhiḥ ityatra  kāyikakarmāṇiyathāupahāradānamukhaprakṣālanādīni
yāni premamayahṛdayānupreritāni 
hitakarāṇi  ityatra tāni karmāṇi ucyante yāni magalavardhanāya kriyante 
sukhāvahāni  ityatrāśayaḥ  karmāṇi sukhena ca harṣeṇa ca kriyante
na duḥkhena vā kaṣṭena vā 
advaitāni  aya bhāvaḥ  kati janāḥ kevalamapareṣā samakṣa
na teṣā parokṣam
premamayakāyikakarmādīni sampādayanti 
anye ca kevalamanyeṣā parokṣa
na teṣā samakṣa
kāryāṇi sampādayanti 
kintu sa ānanda eva na vibhajya premamayakarmāṇi sampādayati sma 
evañca tat kṛtāni premamayakāyikakāryāṇi advaitāni savṛttāni 
parimāṇaśūnyāni  asyārthaḥ  parimāṇa vinā 
sa vivakṣati  tava premamayakāyikakāryāṇi parimāṇena atyanta pracurāṇi 
kintu ida jagat atīva sakīrṇam
sattāyāḥ cūḍāpi atihrasvā 
kṣudre sāttvike jagati pracurāṇā karmaṇā sthānābhāvatvāt karmāṇi parimāṇaśūnyāni iti kathyate 
premamayavācikakarmāṇi  atra vācikakarmāṇi ityatra mukhaprakṣālanasamayaghoṣaṇādikarmāṇi sūcyante 
tāni ca kāruṇikacittānupreṣitāni bhavanti 
kiñca yadi ko'pi upadeśavāṇī śrutvā vadati
'mahāśaya
sādhūkta tvayā' iti pramemayavāicikakarmaṇa udāharaṇam 
 premamayamānasikakarmāṇi ityatrāśayaḥ  yathāsamaya śarīrasya yatna kṛtvā sa nibhṛte sthāne upaviśya eva prakāreṇa cintayati  'mamācāryaḥ  
rogāt kleśācca mukto bhavatu 
sa sukhī bhavatu' iti 
dīghanikāyaṭīkā
sumaṅgalavilāsinī 
savādeṣu idamapi likhita yat bhikṣavaḥ teṣā sveṣā madhye premamayakāyikavācikamānasikakarmaṇāmanuśīlana cakruḥ 
gosigaviṣayakakṣudratarasavāde gotamaḥ anuruddha
nandiya kimbila ca sannyāsinaḥ
draṣṭu yayau 
te bhikṣavaḥ gosigasthe udyāne tasthuḥ 
majjhimanikāya  
buddhaḥ sannyāsinaḥ pṛcchati  paryāpta bhikṣābhojya prāpya dugdhajalamiśraṇavadekatra sukhena sthitvā ki te kuśalina iti na vā 
te uttara dadati yat te nāma kuśalinaḥ teṣāñca paryāpta bhikṣābhojyamasti 
anuruddhasya netṛtve te pṛthak pṛthak buddha vadanti yat te dugdhajalamiśravaṇavat sukhena vasanti 
teṣā mate īdṛśaiḥ satīrthaiḥ bhikṣubhiḥ saha vāsaḥ mahān lābha eva 
te parasparahitārtha premamayakāyikavācikamānasikakarmāṇi kurvanti
 teṣā samakṣa ca parokṣam ca anuruddhaḥ anyān janān prati tadīyā bhakti varṇayati  'aha nimnarūpa cintayāmi  mayā kimīdṛśānām mitrāṇā  
sevārtha mama svīya cittamutsṛṣṭam  
kiñca ki me jīvana teṣā sevārthamiti 
mahāśayaḥ asmāka śarīrāṇi khalu pṛthak pṛthak tiṣṭhanti
tathāpi asmāka cittāni niścayena ekatvāpannāni 
' majjhimanikāya 
 anuruddhasya premamayakāyikavācikamānasikakarmaṇā varṇana vistareṇa kathayati ṭīkā  premamayakāyikakarmāṇi  ityatra kāyikakarmāṇi kāruṇikacittatvāt 
apareṣā jñāne vā ajñāne vā
pratyakṣa vā parokṣa vā 
asmin prasamge
apareṣā samakṣa kāyikavācikakarmāṇi tadaiva sambhavanti yadā ko'pi janaḥ aparaiḥ saha vasati 
vaiparītya sambhavati yadi janāḥ pṛthak pṛthak vasanti 
sarvāsu avasthāsu mānasikakarma sambhavati 
tathā hi  anuruddhaḥ paśyati  dau bhikṣū tena saha vasataḥ 
tayoḥ anyataraḥ vahiḥ viśṛkhala parityajyāyāti 
sa cintanena virakti na prakāśayati  'keneda vyavahṛtam  iti 
varam sa tāni vastūni samuddhṛtya yathāsthāna sthāpayati
yathā svaya sa tyajati samuddharati ca 
athavā viṣāyasya upari yatna gṛhṇāti 
etānyeva pareṣā samakṣa premamayakāyikakarmāṇi ucyante 
tathā hi  ko'pi bhikṣuḥ vahirgacchati
tasya śayyā
viṣṭara prayojanīya dravya ca vahiḥ tyajati 
yathānuruddhena purva vyavasthāpitam
tathaiva yadi sa karoti tarhi tasya premamayakāyikakāryāvalī pareṣā parokṣa bhavet 
yadānuruddhaḥ aparagurujanadvayena saha vasati
taddvayena saha madhura sukhakara ca ālapati
tadā tat karma pareṣā samakṣa premamayavācikakarmeti ucyate 
sa yadi taddvaya mitratāsulabhāya saujanyamūlakāya vā ālāpāya niyojayati
tarhi api premamaya vācika karma bhavet 
kiñca sa taddvaya praśna pṛcchati
athavā tayoḥ uttara dadāti  evavidha karmāpi vācika karmetyucyate 
kiñca yadā dvau gurujanau anyatra gacchataḥ tayoḥ anupasthitau sa tayoh guṇān praśasati  'mama priyau bāndhavau
vayovṛddhau nandiyaḥ kimbilaśca eva eva prakāreṇa sadācāraiḥ yuktau 
tau eva evamabhyāsa kurutaḥ' iti 
eva vidha karma pareṣā parokṣa premamayavācikakarmeti ucyate 
premamayamānasikakarma tadaiva sambhavati yadā pareṣāmupasthitau vānupasthitau vā sa cintayati
 mama priyau bāndhavau vayuvṛddhau nandiyaḥ kimbilacca śatrutāyā jaṭilatāyāśca muktau bhavatām 
tau sukhinau bhavatām iti 
mahāśaya asmāka śarīrāṇi khalu pārthakya bhajanti 
yataḥ śarīrāṇi godhūmacūrṇavad vā mṛttikāvadvā cūrṇībhavanti 
tāni kadāpi ekata na bhajanti 
tathāpi asmāka cittāni niścayena ekatva bhajanti 
ayamāśayaḥ  yadā vayamekatra sānnidhya bhajāmaḥ
kadāpi pṛthak pṛthak na tiṣṭhāmaḥ
kadāpi vivāda na kurmaḥ
sarvadā aikamatya poṣayāmaḥ tadā asmāka cittāni ekatva bhajanti 
arthāt cittaikya jāyate 
katha te ātmanā cittāni tyaktvā pareṣā sevāyai niyojayanti 
tathā hi  kasyacit doṣayukta pātramasti 
kasyacidasti malina vastram 
kasyāpi cāsti saskaraṇīya karma 
asyāmavasthāyā doṣayuktapātravān kathayati bandhavaḥ
mama pātra doṣayukta 
ida pakva karaṇīyam iti 
kintu anye na vadanti 'mama prakṣālanayogya vastramasti' iti 
athavā asti me teṣā vastrāṇi prakṣālayanti
pareṣā saskārakarma ca kurvanti 
anyeṣu ekatamenāpi prathamaghoṣaṇāyā sadṛśī sahayogitā sambhavati
'vāndhava
mama vastrāṇi malināni
tāni prakṣālanīyāni iti 
athavā mamoṭaja bhagnadaśā vrajati 
tasya saskāraḥ karttavya iti 
majjhimanikāyaṭīkā
papañcasudanī 
'siṅgāla prati upadeśe' gotamaḥ gṛhastha siṅgālamupadiśati  premamayaśārīrikavācikamānasikakarmabhiḥ parivrājakān brāhmaṇān ca sevasva
teṣā kṛte dvāramunmukta kuru
jīvanadhāraṇāya ca dravya dehīti 
parivrājakā api sahānubhavānuprāṇitāḥ santaḥ pratyupakāra sādhayiṣyanti 
 ṭīkāyāmucyate vistareṇa  premamayakāyikakarmabhiḥ  ityatra kāyikakarmasu kṛteṣu vyaktiḥ yadi premamaya hṛdaya sṛjati tarhi tāni karmāṇi  
premamayānīti  
yadā ko'pi sasārī eva cintayan bauddhamandira gacchati
'aham bhikṣubhiḥ saha ālapāmīti
' tatra ca gatā jalapātra nītvā jala siñcati
bhikṣūṇā pada vā pṛṣṭa vā savāhayati  ityādīni karmāṇi premamayakāyikakarmāṇītyucyate 
yadā ko'pi sasārī paśyati  bhikṣavo bhikṣārtha grāma praviśantīti
sa ca vadati śraddhayā tebhyaḥ anna vā dugdha vā bhojya vā dehīti
tadā eva vidhāni karmāṇi premamayavācikakarmāṇītyucyate 
kiñca yadā sa śraddhayāntarikatayā ca dharma śṛṇoti
vadati ca 'sādhūkta tvayā' tadā evavidhāni karmāṇi premamayavācikakarmāṇiti kathyate 
yadā kaścit gṛhasthaḥ cintayati
'asmāka sasāram āśritya ye gurujanāstiṣṭhanti te śatrutvāt tathā utpātāt muktā bhavantu
' tadā evavidha vacana kāruṇikahṛdayaprasūtakarma ucyate 
dīghanikāyaṭīkā 
bhavacakrān mahāparinirvāṇasavāde gotamaḥ bhikṣumupadiśati  ṣaṭ avasthāḥ santi  yābhiḥ lābho jāyate 
dīghanikāya 
tathā hi  pareṣā samakṣā vā parokṣa vā satīrthebhyaḥ bhikṣubhyaḥ prītiyukktakāyikavācikamānasikakarmasampādanam
satīrtheṣu bhikṣuṣu bhikṣālabdha dravya vibhajya grahaṇam
sadācāraiḥ vyavahāraḥ
ekāntataḥ duḥkhavināśāya matapoṣaṇam 
buddha āha  yāvatte uktadaśāṣṭaka pālayanti
tāvanniścita te unnataye kalpante 
ṭīkāyā vyākhyāyate  prītisnigdhakāyikakarmāṇi tānyeva yāni kāruṇikena hṛdayena kriyante 
evameva karuṇābhayamanaḥsādhya vācika karma premamayamiti kathyate 
karuṇāmaya manaḥsādhya mānasika karma premamayamityucyate 
asmin pāṭhe īdṛśī karmasamaṣṭiḥ sannyāsinā kṛte nirdiśyate 
tathāpi gṛhastho'pi tādṛśa karma kartumarhati 
karuṇāmayahṛdayenānupreritāḥ santaḥ sannyāsinaḥ yadā sadācāra sādhayanti tadā tat karma prītisnigdhakāyikakarmetyucyate 
yadā gṛhasthā janāḥ śraddhāpradarśanārtha avaśiṣṭādhāra gacchanti
athavā bodhivṛkṣa gacchanti
dharmasampradāya nimantrayitu yānti
bhikṣārtha grāmamāgacchanta bhikṣumālokya ta draṣṭu gacchanti
teṣā bhikṣāpātra gṛṇhanti
upaveśanārtha tān anurundhanti
taiḥ saha gacchanti
tadā evavidhāni karmāṇi prītisnigdhakāyikakarmāṇītyucyate 
yadā sannyāsinaḥ kāruṇikacittānupreritāḥ santaḥ sada cāramupadiśanti
dhyānaviṣaya vyākhyayā vadanti
dharmamupadiśanti
tadā etāni karmaṇi prītisnigdhavācikakarmāṇi ityucyate 
kiñca bauddhadharmaśāstra tripiṭaka nāma 
tatra buddhasya śabdāḥ santi praśnottararūpāḥ 
ida śāstra premamayavācika karma 
gṛsthānā prītisnigdhāvācikakarmāṇi tadaiva bhavanti yadā vadanti
'vaya śraddhāpradarśanārthamaviśiṣṭādhāra gacchāmaḥ 
' vaya pūjārtha bodhivṛkṣa gacchamaḥ' 
'vaya śravaṇīyadharma śrotumavasara racayāmaḥ' 
'dīpaiḥ mālyaiḥ puṣpaiśca pūjā karavāma 
' 'vaya sadabhyāsatraya nirvāhayāmaḥ 
' sadācāraḥ samādhiḥ jñātam 
'vaya yathocitakhādyādi vitarāmaḥ 
' 'varṣartau nibhṛtavāsarātāya bhikṣave upāyana yacchāmaḥ 
' 'adya ādhyātmikasampradāyavyavahṛta dravyacatuṣṭaya paridhāna
bhikṣāpātra śayyā
auṣadha ca yacchāmaḥ 
' 'ādhyātmikasampradāya nimantrayāmaḥ teṣā kṛte ca kaṭhina bhojya sādhayāmaḥ 
' 'upaveśanārtha tān āsana darśaya 
' 'tebhyaḥ jala dehi' 'gaccha
bhikṣūn paśya
taiḥ saha anugaccha 
' 'upayukte viṣṭare upaveśanāya tān sāhāyya kuru 
' 'yathotsāha yathāśakti ca tān sevasva 
' evamanyatrāpi budhyate 
yadā bhikṣavaḥ pratyūṣe utthāya dehasādhanānte avaśiṣṭādhārasamīpa prakṣānārtha yānti
prathāgatakṛtyāni samyādayanti
viviktasthāne upaviśya cintayanti  'bauddhamandirasya sannyāsinaḥ sukhinaḥ bhavantu 
te śatrutāyāstathā jaṭilatāyāśca muktā bhavantu 
' ityevavidha teṣā karuṇāmayamānasikakarma 
yadā gṛhasthāścintayanti
'mahānto janāḥ sukhino bhavantu 
te vairāt upadravācca muktā bhavantu' tadā ityeva teṣā karuṇātmakamānasikakarma 
yadā bhikṣavaḥ paridheyavasanādinirmāṇāya navadīkṣitān sāhāyya kartu gacchanti
tadā tat karma pareṣāmupasthitau prītisnigdhaśārīrikakarmeti ucyate 
api ca gurujanapādaprakṣālana śraddhayā abhyarthanājñāpanamityādīni karmāṇi pareṣā samakṣa prītisnigdhadaihikakarmāṇi ityucyate 
yadā dīkṣiteṣu navīnā vā prācīnā vā dārumayadravyādīni vahiḥ viśṛkhala parityajya anyatra gacchanti
tadā kaścidbhikṣuḥ tāni dravyāṇi suśṛkhala sthāpayati viraktiprakāśa na kṛtvaiva 
sa manyate yat ukta karma tasya svasyeva karma 
evavidha karma apareṣāmanupasthitau premamayakāyikakarmetyucyate 
' agraja deva
agraja tissa' ete śraddhāsūcakāḥ śabdāḥ pareṣā samakṣa premamayavācikakarmaṇā dyotakāḥ 
bauddhamandire agrajadevasya agrajatissasyānupasthitau ko'pi bhikṣuryadi eva vadati  'asmākamagrajaḥ devaḥ kutra gataḥ
kutra gataḥ vā agrajaḥ tissaḥ 
kadā tau pratyāgamiṣyataḥ 
' tadā eṣā uktiḥ pareṣā parokṣa kāruṇikavācikakarmeti ucyate 
vaya yadā prītisnigdhaiḥ locanaiḥ aparān drakṣyāmaḥ
tadā tat karma pareṣāmupasthitau premamayamānasikakarma 
yadi cintyate 'agrajaḥ devaḥ agrajaḥ tissaḥ ca pīḍāyāḥ ca asvāsthyāt ca muktau bhavatām 
' tarhi etādṛśa cintana pareṣāmupasthitau premamayakarmeti ucyate 
dīghanikāyaṭīkā 
iya ṭīkā varṇayati  'kāruṇikacittānupreritāḥ santaḥ bhikṣavaḥ yadā yathāyathamācaranti tadā tat karma premamayakāyikakarmetyucyate iti 
kāruṇyasaujanyayoḥ miśraṇamullekhārham 
theravādīvyākhyānādidamāyāti yat maṅgalamaye manasi vicitraviṣayāṇāmadbhuta miśraṇa jāyate 
hitasādhaka kāruṇika manaḥ katibhiḥ mānasikaiḥ guṇaiḥ anvita tiṣṭhati
