saralonmukhitā ca 
' yathāyathamācaraṇāyānupreraṇāśaktitvena vivecanā lajjā ca hitasādhakacitteṣu vartete ityucyate 
vivecanā ca lajjā ca snāyavika doṣa na sūcayataḥ kintu upayuktavyavahārapravarttakaguṇān sūcayataḥ 
tatra yathākrama vyavahartuḥ svīyaruciḥ athavā pareṣā ruciḥ kārya karoti 
visuddhimagga 
snāyavikadoṣakaraṇādvātmavidveṣādvādūre vartamānaḥ śuddhasaujanyabodhaḥ tayoranupasthiteḥ upari nirbhara karoti 
yadā kaścijjana ātmavidveṣa poṣayati athavā pāpavyākulatāmanubhavati
tadā sa vivekena lajjayā vā śūnyaḥ jāyate 
visuddhimagga  
yataḥ asmin samaye sa svapakṣe parapakṣe vā yathāyatha hitakara kārya na karoti 
yataḥ upayuktanītisammatavyavahāraḥ ātmavidveṣādidoṣebhyo muktena saujanyabodhena pravartito bhavati
tataḥ nītisammata jñāna tathācaraṇa prakṣobhajakleśamantareṇa sambhavati 
 mānasika sāmya namanīyatva laghutvamātmavidveṣādiduṣṭabhāvapariharaṇameteṣā prasage āgativinayamavalambya kaścijjanaḥ viśuddhavyavahāra  
kartu śikṣate  
vyavahāre kasyacinnarasya bhrame lakṣite bhramasvīkaraṇena ca viśuddhīkaraṇecchayā ca pratikāro vidhīyate
na snāyavikapīḍanena 
asmin prasage
vivekaśca lajjā ca aparahitasādhakamānasikaguṇaiḥ saha virodha na bhajataḥ 
teṣu guṇeṣu karuṇāpi vartate 
karuṇayā saha sarve ete guṇāḥ viśuddhavyavahāreṇa saha virājante 
kintu tatra bindumātraḥ kopo'pi na tiṣṭhati
na pāpam
na vā amanamanīyatā 
karuṇā vivecanā
lajjā ca mānasikasukhabodhāya samamanobhāvāya vā sampadyante 
visuddhimagga 
evañca sadācāraḥ karuṇayā ānandena ca saha virājate 
savādeṣu karuṇāmayakāryāvalī samaṣṭigatabhāvena kevala dharmācaraṇakāriṇā kṛte ālocyate 
tatra buddhaḥ ānandaḥ anuruddhaḥ kimbilaḥ nandiyaḥ ityādīnā parasparasavādo'sti 
tatra karuṇāsamṛddhakarmasampādanāya sannyāsinaḥ prati buddhasyopadeśo vartate 
yataḥ etādṛśa karma teṣāmunnataye bhavati 
kāruṇikakarmabhiḥ parivrājakānā ca viprāṇā ca sevārtha sigala prati tasyopadeśo'sti 
atra hetuḥ  parivrājakāśca viprāśca sahānubhūtiśīlāḥ santaḥ tameva upakariṣyanti 
savādeṣu ālocitānā karuṇāsiktakarmaṇā pradhānāḥ kartāraḥ hi bhikṣavaḥ 
tathāpi idamapi avaśyameva gamyate yat sādhāraṇā janā api bhikṣūṇā viśuddha vyavahāra tathā upadeśa gṛhītvā upakṛtā bhaviṣyanti
bhikṣūn prati kāruṇikakarmopadeśānā kaściddoṣaḥ api dṛśyate 
tathā hi  te sādhāraṇajanebhyaḥ kāruṇikakarmalābhāya pralubdhā bhavitumarhanti 
atra buddhasya kaṭhora vidhānamasti yat bhikṣavaḥ yathāyatha bhikṣālabdha dravya bhuñjīran 
ye kāruṇikakarmāṇi labhante
te avaśyameva sukha prāpnuvanti 
ata ea hitakarakāruṇikacittena anuprāṇitāḥ santaḥ janāḥ pramamayakāyikavācikamānasikakarmāṇi kartu pravattante 
etāni karmāṇi sampādayantaḥ abyāsakāriṇaḥ tasmin kṣaṇe eva cittānuṣaṅga sukhamanubhavanti 
kramikānuśāsaneṣu praśasanīyaphalaṣaṭka varṇita buddhena 
yat sarvavidhasāpekṣavyāpāreṣu sannyāsisamīpe duḥkhabodhanivṛttaye bhavati 
aguttaranikāya 
tathā hi   nirvāṇopalabdhiḥ sarvavidhasāpekṣavyāpāreṣu sthāpitā bhaviṣyati 
 manaḥ sarvadeśād vimukha bhaviṣyati 
 sannyāsī nirvāṇarūpā śānti drakṣyati 
 mālinya tathā punarjanma iti sahajātā pravaṇatā dūra gabhiṣyati 
 sannyāsinaḥ sarvakarmaṇā samāptiḥ bhavati 
 sannyāsī kāruṇikakarmaṇā guru sevitu śakṣyati 
śabdāntaramavalambyocyate
sarvavidhasāpekṣavyāpāreṣu duḥkhabodhajāgaraṇāt sannyāsī yathā arhatpuruṣo bhaviturmahati tasya lābhāḥ jāyante 
'karuṇāayakarma ityasya viśleṣaṇa karoti ṭīkā  karuṇāmayakarmabhiḥ karuṇānvitasevābhiḥ
yasmāt saptavidhā śikṣārthinaḥ karuṇāmayakarmabhiḥ sadaikyavanta sevante 
yena bhikṣuṇā hānikarāḥ prabhāvā vinaṣṭāḥ sa sampūrṇakāruṇikakarmabhiḥ ācārya sevate 
' aguttaranikāyaṭīkā 
śikṣārthinaḥ vā aparejanā vā mārgābhijñatā labhante 
tathā ca 'srotaḥpraveśinaḥ' 'sakṛdagāminaḥ' 'anāgāminaḥ' 'anāgāminaḥ' arjjanasya mārgasya viṣayamadhikṛtya jñānamarjayanti
tathāpi te sampūrṇa karuṇāmayakarmabhiḥ guru na sevante 
kintu sampūrṇo muktaḥ puruṣaḥ arhajjanasya sukhāsvāda prāpya guru karuṇāmayakarmabhi sevate 
sarvavidhasāpekṣavyāpāreṣu duḥkhātmakaprakṛtiḥ asti 
tadviṣayakasampūrṇabodhāt sa punaḥ punaḥ punarjanmane ākāṅkṣā dūrīkaroti 
sa sāpekṣavyāpārāṇāmanityatva cāsāratva ca upalabhate 
tasmāt sa punareva kutrāpi āsakti na darśayati athavā tatra ghṛṇāmapi na prakāśayati 
sa sarvavidhakṣyatikaraprabhāvānā vināśakaroti 
ete prabhāvāḥ etāvatkāla tasya citte āsan 
kintu teṣā nāśāt sa sampūrṇa nirvāṇasukhamanubhavati 
sa karuṇāmayakarmabhiḥ guru sevitumalapityucyate 
evamatra 'karuṇāmayakarma' antardṛṣṭi nirdiśati
yā mānasikadūṣaṇāt nara cita mukta karoti 
 tathā ca 'kṣudratarachoṭikā'viṣayikī ṭīkā vadati  yadā sannyāsī pratyakṣajñānagamya viṣaya pratyakṣa jānāti tadā sa premamaya manaḥ poṣayati 
 yadyapīda gabhirāntardṛṣṭidvārā  nirvāṇopalabdhidvārā prema sṛjati tathāpi sāmānyārthayuktā karuṇā asmin prasage na āyāti  dhammapālena  
tadīyaṭīkāyā viśuddhimārga vyākhyāsu viśadārtha prakaṭitaḥ  
 premakaruṇādayaḥ ye mānasikaguṇā indriyavadbhiḥ prāṇibhiḥ saha sambandha sthāpayanti te viṣayatvena na āyānti yadā dhyāninaḥ manaḥ nirvāṇa  
labhate  
 kramikānuśāsanebhyaḥ uddhṛtasya prāguktasyānucchedasya ālocanāyām sāntardṛṣṭikaruṇāyāḥ rūpakāśrita samīkaraṇa sūcayati yat sadṛśabhāvāpannaḥ  
vyavahāraḥ kṣudratarachoṭikāṭīkāyāmasti  
yā paravarttinī ṭīkā dhammapālasyābhimatena saha sagatisampannā karoti 
ṭīkā anusṛtya kathyate yat premamayī karuṇā paryāyatraye'vatiṣṭhate 
tathā hi  prāthamikaparyāye
praveśaparyāye
samādhiparyāye ca 
tathāpi 'karuṇāyāḥ' uparyukta rūpakāśrita vyavahāramantareṇa
 savādeṣūllikhitāḥ sarve karuṇāsamparkitadṛṣṭāntāḥ niḥsaśaya vā sasaśaya vā samādheḥ praveśaparyāyasya athavā sthāpanāūlakaparyāyasya ca  
śaktyā saha virājante  
ida karuṇātmakatāyāḥ ca karuṇāyāḥca prayoge pārthakya karoti 
dvitīyā mānasiīmavasthā sūcayati yā karuṇāśakti dhārayati  prāthamikaparyāyāt sthāpanāparyāya yāvat 
kramikānuśāsaneṣu gotamaḥ bhikṣūṇupadiśati yat karuṇayā vā mānasamuktyā vā saha tulanīya na karmāpi viṣaya sa paśyati 
karuṇāyāḥ krodhapratirodhasāmarthyamasti
krodhadūrīkaraṇasāmarthyamapi asti 
aguttaranikāya 
gotamaḥ bhikṣūn āha  yadi te muktipradhānā karuṇā prati sayatna manoyoga dadati
tarhi krodho na jāyate athavā jātaḥ krodho'pi dūra gacchati 
ṭīkāyāmucyate prītiḥ katha manasaḥ muktiḥ bhavitumarhati 
manasaḥ muktirhi prītiḥ tathā karuṇā 
eṣā eva karuṇā maṅgalakāmanayā indriyavadbhiḥ jīvaiḥ sahaḥ sambandhatvāt 
kiñca yataḥ sakaruṇa manaḥ pratibandhakādiviruddhaguṇebhyaḥ mukta bhavati
tataḥ aya vyāpāraḥ manasaḥ muktiriti kathyate 
nirdiśya kathyate
kruddhajanasyāpi karuṇāyā sañjātāyā manasaḥ muktiḥ bhavati 
asmin prasage
kiyatā parimāṇena iyameva karuṇā tasyāḥ prāthamika rūpamapi viṣayopayogi 
tathāpyatra
'manaso muktiḥ' iti kathanena sa kevala karuṇāsthāpanāparyāya sūcayati 
aguttaranikāyaṭīkā 
yadi kaścijjanaḥ vipado'pareṣāmuddhārāya karaṇatva vrajati tarhi sa teṣā 'muktiḥ' ityucyate 
atra hetureva phalam 
evañca yadā karuṇā yathārīti dhyānamagnatāyai kṛṣyate
iya niścayena nivāraṇebhyaḥ manaḥ mocayati 
yataḥ krodhānmanaso muktaye karuṇāyā viśiṣṭā paṭutāsti
tata iya phalanāma prāpnoti
'manaso muktiḥ' 
prathamā nimagnatā nivāraṇebhyo muktā 
asyāḥ pañca mukhyāni upādānāni santi 
tathā hi  vastuni prāthamikamanaḥsayogaḥ vitakka
 vastuni manoyogasthāpanam vicāra
 prītiḥ pīti
sukham sukha
 samādhiḥ samādhi ca 
visuddhimaggaḥ 
gabhīraḥ samādhiḥ atyantamānandaḥ ceti anayoḥ miśraṇena mānasikī daśā asvābhāvikī iti dṛśyate 
svābhāvikīṣu avasthāsu
yadā eko naro manaḥsayoga karoti
tadā etāvanniṣpeṣaṇa tiṣṭhati yat paramasukha na sambhavati 
 prāthamikanimagnatālābhāya vinayanavyāpāre sā śikṣā kriyate yatra praceṣṭāyāḥ śaktiḥ ca samādheḥ sthiratā ca ityanayoḥ madhye samatā sthāpyate 
phalataḥ tīvrasya atha ca udvegamuktasya manasaḥ samādhiḥ sambhavati 
asyāmavasthāyā paramasukhasya navīnābhijñatā jāyate 
yathāyathasamādhaye samatāsampannapraceṣṭayā prayojanamasti 
tatprakṛtiviśleṣaṇāya viśuddhimārge buddhaghoṣaḥ eka sundara dṛṣṭānta dadāti 
bhāratīyāḥ śalyavidaḥ jale bhāsamāneṣu padmapatreṣu śalyakriyākaraṇāya śikṣā dadati 
visuddhimagga 
atyutsāhī śikṣārthī tatpatra nimagna karoti athavā tatpatra sampūrṇa dvidhā kṛntati 
bhītipravaṇastu padmapatre balasya prayogāya samartho na bhūtvā tatpatrakarttanāya vyartho bhavati 
atra saphalasya śikṣārthinaḥ samatāsampannā śaktirasti 
sa padmapatra nimagna na kṛtvāpi tatpatra sampūrṇa karttitumarhati 
evañca samādhilābhapraceṣṭā samatāsampannā bhavet 
tatra atyudvegastathā atigurutā na sthāsyati
punaśca
na sthāsyati atilaghutā tathā svapnālutā 
samarūpasampannasamādhilābhāya vinayaśca yatnaśca karaṇīyau 
ata eva paramasukhena saha muktapremāsvādaḥ durlabhaḥ 
mānasikaviṣayadhyānakāle 'prāthamikamanaḥsayogaḥ' vitakka
samabhāvenaiva dhyānagatavastuṣu manasaḥ ca ānuṣagikamānasikaviṣayāṇā ca sthāpana karoti 
samādheḥ asmin paryāye idameva eṣā mānasikānā viṣayāṇāmapūrva vaiśiṣṭyam 
pratyuta āsaktiḥ mānasavastūni ākarṣati 
visuddhimagga 
kiñca āsaktiḥ sarvadā vyākulatayā saha vartate yatra vihvalatāyāḥ prāvaṇya dṛśyate 
āsaktyā sthāyihatāśābodhaḥ saśliṣyate
yata āsaktyāḥ sadāvarttamānā sahacarī vyākulatā sābhiprāyamilanasādhakalakṣyasya upalabdhaye pratibandhakatā sṛjati 
prāthamikamanaḥsayogasya vitakka
'sthāpanam' appana
iti ākhyāpi tiṣṭhati 
yasmāt vastuṣu manaḥsthāpanaśaktirasya vartate 
majjhimanikāya  
tathāpi manasaḥ ca mānasaviṣayāṇā a dhyānamagnatāśaktirasti tataḥ
manasā saha te sarve viṣayāḥ sthāpanābhidhānena viśiṣyante 
evamuparyuktāyā ṭīkāyām
'sthāpanā' appana
dhyānamagnatāparyāyagatakaruṇā sūcayati yatra sadṛśī śaktirasti 
manomuktisādhanāya karuṇāyai vā dhyāninā puruṣeṇa avalambanīyāḥ paryāyā visuddhimagge vistareṇālocitāḥ 
maḥ adhyāyaḥ
samāsataḥ poṣa gatāyāḥ karuṇāyāḥ sāmānyīkaraṇārtha tathā niviḍatāpādanārtha paddhatistatra varṇitā 
navadīkṣita ātmāna gṛhītvaiva sādhanāmārgābhimukha gantumarabhate 
sa icchati 'aha sukhī bhavāni
aha varānmukto bhavāni' iti 
tataḥ sa yathā sukhī bhaviṣyatīti kāmayate
tathā anye'pi kāmayante iti avabudhya sa svabhāvataḥ apareṣā maṅgala kāmayate 
tataḥ sa priyadharmaguruṣu anyatamāya karuṇā poṣayitum ārabhate 
idamucyate yat abhyāsakārī tadīyagurudevasya utsāhavardhaka priya vākya smṛtvā
praśasanīyavyavahāram dṛstvā
upayuktaśikṣaṇa prāpya ca anāyāsenaiva tasmai karuṇārpaṇāya samartho bhavati 
tataḥ abhyāsakārī paryāyakrameṇa priyamitrāya karuṇārpaṇāya ceṣṭate 
navadīkṣitānā kṣetre viparītaliṅgatā parityājyā
tathā ca ceṣṭate nirapekṣajanāya ca śatrumanobhāvāpannajanāya cāpi 
ayamāśayaḥ  sa sarveṣu janeṣu karuṇāyā vistārāya tadīyacitta sampūrṇa namanīya dakṣa ca sādhayati 
atreda sambhavati yat abhyāsakārī śatrubhāvāpanna janamanusmṛtya ātmani śatrutā poṣaiṣyati
asya pratirodhāya
jātavairasya anyatra sthāpanāya tathā tat sambhāvanāhrāsāya buddhaghoṣaḥ katividhān vimarśān kathayati 
atra eṣu vimarśadayamālocyate 
prathamataḥ
naraḥ tadīyakarmaphalamuttarādhikārāt prāpnoti 
visuddhimagga 
abhyāsakārī yadi vaira poṣayati tarhi sa paryavekṣate yat sa tatkṣaṇāt vidveṣamiśrita mānasika duḥkha prāpnoti 
visuddhimagga 
punaśca sa bhaviṣyati adhikataravairasṛṣṭaye hetūnāviskaroti 
tasmāt maraṇāt para duḥkhamayapunarjanma yathā bhavati tathā ca vyāhatā bhavati ādhyātmikasamṛddhiḥ 
atra sa yadi vaira tyajati
tarhi sa svaya vidveṣamiśritaānasikakaṣṭāt mukto bhaviṣyati 
kiñca sa bhaviṣyati svalpavairasṛṣṭaye hetūn sṛjati 
tena tasya punarjanma sukhakara bhavati
ādhyātmikī samṛddhirapi bhavati 
api ca yadyapi kaścid vairī uparyuktaiḥ sarvaiḥ upāyaiḥ abhyāsakāriṇamapakarttu yāti
tathāpi vairijana prati pratihisā na karttavyā 
yataḥ kaścit janaḥ aparasya yatparimāṇamapakāramicchati tadapekṣayādhikatara duḥkha sa prāpnoti
prāpsyati ca pratītyasamutpādatatasya prabhāvāt 
dvitīyataḥ
naitādṛśaḥ ko'pi janaḥ yaḥ kasmisicit samaye kasyāpi na mātā pitā bhaginī bhrātā vā bhavati 
visuddhimagga 
yasmāt punarjanma asmāka paścāt anirdiṣṭakāla vitatya tiṣṭhati
tasmāt adya pṛthivyā na ko'pi janaḥ asti yo'smāka niviḍa sambandha nāgataḥ 
asmāka mātṛrūpeṇa yā vyaktiḥ ekadā asmān tasyāḥ aṅke sthāpayitvā
āpattiśūnyānasmān pariṣkṛtya
sarvavidhamapacaya svīkṛtya asmān sayatna pālayāmāsa
atha ca tā prati adhunā vaya śatrutā poṣayāmaḥ 
pitṛrūpeṇāya janaḥ asmāka pālanāya dīrdha kāla kaṭhora śrama cakāra 
asmāka bhaginīrūpeṇa vā bhrātṛrūpeṇa vāya jano vividhaiḥ upāyaiḥ asmāka sahāyatā jagāma 
evam etādṛśa jana prati vaira na karttavyam
yataḥ atīte kāle sa janaḥ asmāka kṛte upakāra cakāra 
evavidhābhiścintābhiḥ manaḥsayogāt abhyāsakārī śatrujana prati karuṇāpoṣaṇakāle jātakrodhasyānyatra sthāpanāya paṭutaraḥ jāyate 
śatrutāyā vināśa kṛtvā tathā kāścit mānasikī samatā prāpya abhyāsakārī ta prati karuṇā pālayitum agrasaro bhavitumarhati 
yā karuṇā sa ātmane anubhavati
gurudevāya
nirapekṣajanāya cānubhavati sā karuṇaiva asmai janāya karttavyā abhyāsakāriṇā janena 
eva so'bhyāsakārī eteṣā viṣayamadhikṛtya karuṇāsakrāntā tīvrāmabhijñatāmavaśyameva racayet 
tataśca sa śatrujana prati karuṇā nayati 
anena abhyāsena dhyānī puruṣasḥ svabhāvata eva sarvajīvahitecchayā karmāṇi ācaritu yatate 
yadi abhyāsakārī ātmani
priyamitre
nirapekṣajane
śatrāvapi karuṇā pālayitu saphalo bhavati
tarhi tena ātmaparabhedabādhaḥ bhagnaḥ jātaḥ iti ucyate 
visuddhimagga 
aya vyāpāraḥ praveśaparyāyagatakaruṇālābha sūcayati 
tataḥ abhyāsakārī karuṇāyāḥ sthāpanaparyāya yāti 
tena karuṇā gabhīrā ca ekaniṣṭhā ca bhavati 
tatra praveśakṣamā śaktirasti ityucyate 
tataḥ abhyāsakārī tathārīti karuṇāyāḥ parisaramāgatānā jīvānā sakhyā vardhayati 
tathā ca sa uttarottara sārvalaukika paryāya yāvat karuṇā netu yatate 
sagotrīyavacaneṣu ātmā manibhaddaḥ gotama prati śloka vadati  manasvī janaḥ sarvadā bhāgyavān 
manasvī janaḥ sukha paśyati 
manasvijanāya āgāmikalya sundarataram 
sa vairāt pramucyate 
sayuttanikāya 
gotamaḥ prativadati  manasvī janaḥ sarvadā bhāgyavān 
manasvī janaḥ sukha paśyati 
manasvijanāya āgāmikalya sundarataram 
sa vairānna pramucyate 
sa hānihīnatāyā nandati samagra divasa samagrā rajanī ca sa sarveṣu jīveṣu snihyati 
tasya kasyopari vaira nāsti 
sayuttanikāya 
gotamasya ślokā nirdiśanti yat yo jano manasvitāyāḥ anuśīlana karoti sa vairāt na mukto bhavati 
kintu yo janaḥ hānihīnatāyā nandati sarvadā
sarveṣu jīveṣu ca snihyati sa vairānmukto jāyate 
kasyacijjanasya cintā tiṣṭhati aha manasvīti 
kiyatā parimāṇena iti na viṣayaḥ 
sa vairāt na mukto bhaviṣyati iti ṭīkā svīkaroti 
sayuttanikāyaṭīkā 
ṭīkā viśliṣyati yat buddhenoccārite dvitīye padye uddiṣṭo janaḥ arhatpuruṣaḥ 
sa prema ca karuṇā ca manasi pālayati 
sa eva vairāt mukto bhavati 
asyāḥ ṭīkāyāḥ ko'rtha 
viśuddhimārgamanusṛtya kathyate yat manasvitā sāvadhānatā vā hitakaro mānasikaḥ viṣayaḥ 
visuddhimagga 
ṭīkāsu aya niścayo savitarkamucyate kasmiścidupaṭīkāyām
yat hitakaramānasikaviṣayāḥ ahitakaramānasikaviṣayaiḥ saha sthātu na śaknuvanti 
 yadā manasvitā vā sāvadhānatā vā ityākhyaḥ hitakaro mānasiko viṣayaḥ asthāyibhāvena upasthitastiṣṭhati tadā ko'pi ahitakaro mānasiko viṣayo  
na tatra sthātum arhati  
eva yadi abhyāsakārī purvatanakrodhamuhūrtta cintayati
tarhi tasya manaḥ varttamāne muhūrtte svabhāvata eva krodhānmukta bhavati 
sa hitakaramanoyuktaḥ yadā bhavati tadā sa trayodaśamānasikaguṇaiḥ anvitastiṣṭhati 
te sarvadā hitakaramanasā saha varttante 
tathā hi  pratyayaḥ
sāvadhānatā
vivekaḥ
lajjā
ghṛṇāśūnyatā
nirlobhatā
samaprāṇatā
śāntacittatā
laghutā
namanīyatā
dakṣatā
viśeṣajñatā ṛjutā 
visuddhimagga 
saḥ anubhavadvayasya ekatarasyābhijñatā labhate 
tathā hi mānasika sukha samavṛttitā ca 
etau anubhavau hitakaramanasā anvitau tiṣṭhataḥ 
visuddhimagga 
yo'bhyāsakārī manasvitā sāvadhānatā vā poṣayati
sa bhaviṣyati kāle sadṛśī hitakarī pravaṇatā sṛjati
īdṛśasya janasya kṛte 'āgāmikalya sundarataram' iti 
tathāpi gotamasya mate
manasvitayā śatrutāyāḥ anyatra sthapana na paryāptam
manasvī sāvadhānī vā janaḥ śatrutāyā muktaḥ na bhavati 
anyeṣu prasageṣu karuṇā mānasamuktiriti kathyate 
atra hetuḥ  dhyānamagnatāparyāye mānasamuktau satyā sā muktiḥ alpakāla manaḥ krodhamukta karoti 
aguttaranikāya ṭīkā  maḥ 
yo'bhyāsakārī dhyānamagnatāparyāya vyāpya dakṣatayā karuṇā poṣayati
sa svaya krodhamukto jāyate 
tathā ca dhyānamagnatayā saha paramasukha bhuñkte 
 api ṭīkākārāḥ gotamoktaślokasya nimnarūpā vyākhyā kurvanti tathā hi  vairibhāvāt yathāyatha mānasamuktisādhanāya karuṇā dhyānamagnatayā  
poṣayitavyā  
eṣā sambhāvanā parityaktu śakyate 
yataḥ manasvitā anyatra sthāpanena manaḥ kevala svalpakāla vairāt mukta karoti 
eṣā manasvitā na vairāt santoṣāvahā muktiḥ 
evameva karuṇā avadamanena svalpakāma mānasamukti sādhayati 
eṣāpi vairāt santoṣāvahā muktiḥ bhavitu nārhati 
ṭīkā tu pṛthagbhāvamavalambate 
 ṭīkā vyākhyāti yat prathame śloke uddiṣṭaḥ janaḥ adhunāpi 'aha manasvī vā sāvadhānī vā' iti cintayā manasvitānuśīlana karoti sayuttanikāya 
tena na ātmano'sārā prakṛtiḥ upalabdhā 
sa nopalabdhi karoti yat
manasvitānuśīlane
sāpekṣaviṣayaḥ aparasāpekṣaviṣaya paśyati visuddhimagga 
sa nopalabdhi karoti yat kevalamanityā mānasikāḥ śārīrikāśca padārthā vartante 
tatra kasmiścidapi padārthe na cirasthāyī ātmā dṛśyate 
īdṛśo janaḥ bhrānta mata
padacetanāmākāṅkṣā ca na nirākartu śaknoti visuddhimagga 
sa āśābhagnaḥ sañjātavairāt na mukto bhavitumarhati 
dvitīye śloke uddiṣṭo janaḥ abhyāsakārī
sampūrṇamuktārhatpuruṣa iti vyākhyāyate 
sa sarvavidhasāpekṣavastūnāmanityatva pratyakṣīkaroti 
so'nubhavati yat paramārthataḥ nityaḥ sārabhūtaḥ ca 'aham' nāsti
yo'ha daihikabhūteṣu manasi vā sarvatra dṛśyate 
saḥ 'ahamasmi' ahamasmi mamansvī'  evavidhayā cintayā na punaḥ baddhaḥ tiṣṭhati 
sayuttanikāya 
arhatpuruṣaḥ vaireṇa saha sarvavidhamānasikadūṣaṇebhyaḥ ātmāna cita moktumarhati 
visuddhimagga  
sa sarvadā prema ca karuṇā ca pālayitumalam 
vairāt tasya muktiḥ paripūrṇā 
krakacadṛṣṭāntasavāde gotamaḥ vividhāsu avasthāsu kāruṇikacittalālanena prayojanamupadiśati 
majjhimanikāya 
buddhaḥ bhikṣūnāha yat teṣā sambodhana pañcadhā bhaviṣyati 
tathā hi  upayuktasamaye athavā anupayuktasamaye
satyamanusṛtya athavā asatyamanusṛtya
kārkaśyena athavā mādhuryeṇa
lābhajanakatayā athavā alābhajanakatayā
kāruṇikacittavadbhiḥ athavā krodhayuktaiḥ 
gotamaḥ bhikṣūn jñāpayati yat yenopāyenaiva teṣā sambodhana bhavatu vā na vā
te karuṇāmaya citta pālayeyuḥ 
sa teṣā vinayana viśliṣyati  asmāka cittāni unmārgagāmīni na bhavantu 
vaya kuvākya na vadiṣyāmaḥ 
vaya parebhyaḥ hitāya sahānubhava poṣayiṣyāmaḥ 
asmāka cittāni prītisnigdhāni bhaviṣyanti
krodhamuktāni bhaviṣyanti 
cittagatakaruṇayā vayam āhvāyakena janena saha sambandhasya cheda na kariṣyāmaḥ 
samagra jagadasmāka kāruṇikacittānā gantavya sthalam 
tena jagatā saha asmāka sambandhaḥ dṛḍhaḥ bhavatu 
cittāni bhavantu praśāntāni
vairāt muktāni
viśālāni
vistṛtāni
parimāṇaśūnyāni ca 
majjhimanikāya 
yādṛśī karuṇā bhikṣūṇā tiṣṭhatu tāmeva bhiksavaḥ janāya poṣayet 
tataśca karuṇāyāḥ sāmānyīkaraṇa karttavyam 
ṭīkā yathāśabda vyākhyāti  'samagram' sarvasacetanajīvasametam
'jagat' sacetanānā jīvānā sthānam
'viśālam' yasya viṣayatvena sacetanajīvagaṇastiṣṭhati
'vistṛtam' astitvarakṣāyai vistṛtā bhūmirasti
'parimāṇaśūnyam' yataḥ idamutkṛṣṭam
vairānmuktam krodha vinā
'nirudvignam' duḥkhaśūnyam 
majjhimanikāyaṭīkā 
atra varṇita citta vistṛtam
yasmāt astitvasūcakasamagrabhūmirevāsyādhikāre vartate
rūpamaya tathā rūpahīna jagat 
viśuddhimagga  
yadā citta dhyānamagnatāparyāya yāvat kṛṣṭa bhavati
tadā tat citta jagatparivartana karotīti kathyate 
ida rūpamaya sūkṣmajagat praviśati yadi dhyānamagnātāyāḥ prathamaparyāya  catuṣṭaya vyāpya kṛṣyate 
athavā ida rūpahīna sūkṣmatara jagat praviśati yadi ādhikyena kṛṣyate 
anena jagatā saha anvitasya manasaḥ avasthā vistṛtāḥ 
yataḥ svalpakālamapi dūṣaṇaparihārāya mahat sāmarthyamasti api ca
tatpakṣ mahadupāyanamapi asti 
ṭīkā  yasmāt karuṇā dhyānamagnatāyāḥ ādyaparyāyatraye sthātumarhati visuddhimagga 
tasmāt atra vistṛtapadena trayāṇāmekatama budhyate 
atra prabandhe
karuṇāmaya citta 'parimāṇaśūnya'miti api varṇyate 
sāmānyataḥ
yaḥ samādhiḥ sādhu kṛṣyate tathā dhyānamagnatāyāḥ prathame paryāye tiṣṭhati
anyeṣu paryāyeṣu api
sa samādhiḥ parimāṇaśūnyaḥ iti kathyate 
visuddhimagga 
prathamaparyāyamantareṇāpi uccataraparyāye samādhiḥ etāmākhyā prāpnoti
yataḥ asmin samaye samādhiḥ indriyatṛṣṇādimayajagataḥ sarvavidhasīmāvaddhatābhyaḥ muktaḥ bhavati 
ṭīkā  yā iyam ākhyā dhyānamagnatāparyāyagatasamādhi nirdiśati sā tatraiva paryāye karuṇānvitacitta sūcayati 
evamasmin savāde gotamo bhikṣūnupadiśati yat te dhyānamagnatāparyāya yāvat karuṇā poṣayeyuḥ 
yadi te dhyānena kiyatā parimāṇena  karuṇākarṣaṇe saphalāḥ bhavanti tarhi teṣā cittāni karuṇayā yujyante
sakaruṇaiḥ aparaiḥ guṇaiḥ api visuddhimagga 
dhyānaparavarttisamaye te hitakaracittena saha bhārasāmya sthāpayanti tathā ca mānasika sukha vā samavṛttitva vā anubhavanti 
teṣāmuparodho duḥsādhyaḥ 
krakacadṛṣṭānte gotamaḥ kāruṇikacittasya balasya ca sthāyitvasya ca dṛṣṭānta kathayati 
sa bhikṣūn pṛcchati  ko janaḥ yuṣmāsu khananena vā mūtratyāgena vā pṛthivyā vināśa kartu samarthaḥ bhaviṣyatīti 
neti teṣā prativacanamāsīt 
yasmāt pṛthivī gabhīrā aparimeyā ca appameyya 
tataḥ gotamaḥ pṛthivyāḥ abhedyatā kāruṇikacittasya śaktiḥ ityanayoḥ madhye tulanā pradarśayati 
sa bhikṣūnāha  api ko'pi bhikṣuḥ pañcasu upāyeṣu anyatamamavalambya apareṇa saha ālapet 
api sa premamaya citta pālayet 
athavā api te karuṇārdrahṛdayena aparajanena saha sambandha sthāpayet 
 bhikṣubhiḥ nimnoktopāyena vinayana kartavya  sarvaiḥ jīvaiḥ saha yat jagat tat sarvameva kāruṇikacittasya lakṣyasthala vidhāya vaya cittena  
samagreṇa jagatā saha sambandha sthāpayitumalam  
jagadiveda cittamakṣobha vairānmukta viśāla vistṛta parimāṇaśūnya ca 
majjhimanikāya 
yathā ko'pi janaḥ khanitreṇa ca pātreṇa ca viśālapṛthivīvināśāya na samarthaḥ bhavati
tathā pañcavidhāni vacanāni pratikūlatayā karuṇārdracittavanta jana abhibhavitu na śaknuvanti 
majjhimanikāya 
pṛthivī yathā ākramaṇa nirākaroti gabhīratvāt aparimeyatvāt ca
tathaiva karuṇārdracittam 
tadvat gotamaḥ bhikṣūnapadiśati yat te karuṇā pālayiṣyanti 
tathākaraṇena teṣā cittamakhaṇḍadeśavat avarṇanīya bhaviṣyati
gaṅgāvat bhaviṣyati adahanīyam 
ūrṇāmayakhaṇḍena gharṣaṇāt susyūtaḥ viḍalacarmapuṭaḥ karkaśaḥ na bhavati 
bhiksavo yadi imamupadeśamanusaranti
tarhi teṣā citta sahasā pralubdha
pradīpta karkaśa ca na bhaviṣyati 
sagotrīyavacaneṣu gotama upadiśati yat yasmin gṛhe bahavaḥ strīlokāḥ kintu atyalpāḥ puruṣāstiṣṭhanti
tat gṛhamanāyāsena ākrānta bhavati 
tadvat yo bhikṣuḥ karuṇārūpamanomukti na sādhayati sa niścitamamānuṣībhiḥ śaktibhiḥ upadrutaḥ bhavati 
sayuttanikāya 
anyataśca yasmin gṛhe bahavo narāḥ kintu atyalpā nāryyaḥ tiṣṭhanti
tadgṛha sahasā dasyubhiḥ ākrānta na bhavati
tathā yo bhikṣuḥ karuṇārupamanomukti sādhayati saḥ amānuṣībhiḥ śaktibhiḥ abhibhūtaḥ na bhavati 
tataḥ sa bhikṣūn karuṇānuśīlanāya upadiśati 
savādānā pañcamasagrahe 'karuṇāsavāde' gotamaḥ bhikṣūnupadiśati katha dhyātavyamiti
yena dhyānena duṣṭagrahabhaya na tiṣṭhati
bhikṣavaḥ taiśca upadrutāḥ na bhavanti khuddakapāṭha 
 lābhajanakeṣu abhyāseṣu dakṣaḥ janaḥ ki kuryāt yadā sa śāntipūrṇā daśā jānāti 
sa samarthaḥ
sajjanaḥ
saralo'thaca dṛḍhaḥ
grahaṇakṣamaḥ
namanīyaḥ vinītaḥ
santuṣṭaḥ
sukhena puṣṭaḥ bhavet
svalpakarmabhiḥ svalpavastubhiḥ
samarthaiḥ indriyaiḥ
jñānī karmaṇi vivicya sasāriṇaścānukṛtya sa kadāpi na nīcācaraṇamācaret 
tadācarana jñānijanakartṛkaguṇadoṣavivecana janayati 
sa etāḥ kāmanāḥ pālayet
'sarve jīvāḥ sukha nirbhaya ca vasantu 
te sarve hṛdayena sukhinaḥ bhavantu 
ya eva prāṇavān jīvaḥ
sthiro vā asthiro vā vyatikramamantareṇa
dīrgho'thavā viśālaḥ madhyamo hrasvaḥ sūkṣmo'sūkṣmo vā dṛśyo vā adṛśyo vā
dūravarttī vā nikaṭavartī vā jīvo yo vā janiṣyate te sarve hṛdayena sukhino bhavanti 
ko'pi janaḥ apara jana na pratārayet 
ko'pi janaḥ kasyāpi samīpe kutrāpi ca sammānāt garvito na bhavet 
kenāpi anyajanahānicintā na karaṇīyā 
krodhād vā vidveṣād vā sarvān jīvān prati asīma citta pālayet 
yathā mātā svīyajīvanavyayenāpi ekamātra putra rakṣati 
asīma premamaya citta poṣayet bādha krodha virodha vāntareṇa samagra jagat prati upari
adhaḥ
pārśvāt pārśvāntaram ca 
daṇḍāyamānāvasthāyā
vacaraṇe
upaveśane śayane vā sa manasvitāmavalambya dṛḍhasakalpo bhavet 
atrāyamevodātto bhāvaḥ prakīrtitaḥ 
mithyāmata parihāya satyamācaraṇa tathā satyadṛṣṭimavalambya kāmyavastuṣu āsakti dūrikṛtya sa nūna na navagarbha gamiṣyati 
khuddakapāṭha 
 ṭīkāyā mate yadā bhikṣāvaḥ uktasavādagataviṣayamavagatya tasya upadeśān anusaranti tathā karuṇā poṣayanti tadā vighnakāriṇaḥ devāḥ kamapi  
vighna na sṛṣṭvā santuṣṭāḥ sukhinaḥ sahayoginaḥ sahāyakāśca bhavanti  
khuddakapāṭha 
eva daivaśaktīnāmabhibhavāya karuṇāyāḥ sāmarthyamasti viśākhānāmadheyasya bhikṣoḥ upākhyānenāsya matasya samarthana kriyate
yasya karuṇāśīlanāt amānuṣyaḥ śaktayaḥ tasya sannidhau paraspara śāntipūrṇabhāvena vasanti 
visuddhimagga 
tāḥ śaktayo yadi karuṇānuśīlanakāribhiḥ bhikṣubhiḥ saha sahayogitā na kurvanti
tathāpi tā bhikṣūnapakarttu na śakṣyanti 
sagotrīyavacaneṣu gotamo vadati  yadi amānuṣyaḥ śaktayaḥ karuṇārūpamanomuktisādhanakāriṇā bhikṣūṇām upadrava kurvanti
tadā vā eva pariśrāntā bhaviṣyanti 
sayuttanikāya 
tathāpi abhyāsakārī bhayādvā dāsyād vā amānuṣībhiḥ śaktibhiḥ sṛṣṭādupadravādrakṣaṇa na kāmayate 
vara bhayāsaktigarvādīn doṣān parityajya manomuktirūpakaruṇā karṣati  udāttabhāvam 
aguttaranikāyaṭīkā
 visuddhimagga 
tataḥ tasya citta sthira sāmyāpanna tathā paramasukhamaya bhavati 
viśuddhimagga 
tathā ca tat citta sarvavidhamānasikavipattipratirodhakāri bhavati 
idamucyate yat abhyāsakārī kāyikopadravādapi rakṣyate 
visuddhimagga  
tathā hi  sāmānyā nārī sapavatī gotamasya pradhānā śiṣyā āsīt 
karuṇānuśīlana kurvatī sā karuṇayā svīyahānipratirodhāya samarthā āsīt 
aguttaranikāya 
tasyā ānugatye aviśvāsī san tasyāḥ svāmī vāṇena tā antumudyato'bhavat 
kintu sasakhī samavatī premṇā karuṇayā ca svāmina mugdhamakarot 
ataḥ sa īpsita vadha samāptu na śaśāka 
viśuddhimagga 
tathāpi samavatī svaya vyatikramatva bhajati 
sā karuṇānuśīlane nipuṇā satyapi avaśeṣe tatkṛtahānikarakāryaphalāt agnidāhena amriyata 
abhyāsakāriṇaḥ karuṇā aparajanamanobhāva kalyāṇābhimukha kartu samarthā iti spaṣṭo dṛṣṭāntaḥ savādeṣu yadyapi nāsti
tathāpi karuṇāyā īdṛśī śaktirasti iti viśuddhimārge kathyate 
samādhaye catvāriśadvastuṣu anyatamasya upari yathāyatha dhyātumārabhate abhyāsakārī 
athavā antardṛṣṭisamunnataye yatate 
tasmāt prak sa nimnoktopāyena karuṇā pālayedityupadiśyate 
dhyānaviṣaya gṛhītā bhikṣuḥ prathamataḥ upāsanālayasaśliṣṭānā bhikṣūṇā sampradāyasya sīmā nirdeśet 
tataḥ sa teṣā kṛte evavidhayā cintayā karuṇā pālayet  'te sukhino bhavantu
muktāśca bhavantūpadravāt' iti 
tataḥ sa grāmasthānā devatānā kṛte karuṇā pālayet 
tataḥ sa netṛsthānīyānā janānāmupuri karuṇā poṣayet ye janāḥ tasmai khādyādi dadati 
tataśca sarveṣā manuṣyāṇā tathā jīvānā kṛte karuṇānuśīlana kuryāt 
upāsanālayasaśliṣṭabhikṣūṇā kṛte pālitayā karuṇayā sa tasya sahacareṣu komalahṛdayatā janayati 
te ca ekatra tena saha sukhena vasanti 
upāsanālayasaśliṣṭānā devatānā kṛte pālitayā karuṇayā tā devatāḥ komalahṛdayāḥ satyaḥ yathāyatha rakṣaṇena ta sampūrṇa rakṣanti 
netṛsthānīyānā grāmavāsinā kṛte pālitayā karuṇayā te komalahṛdayāḥ santaḥ yathāyatha sayatna tasmai āvaśyakadravyadānena sevante 
mānavatā kṛte pālitayā karuṇayā te mānavāḥ svacchahṛdayā bhavanti 
tataḥ sa yadā parivrajati tadā te na avajñā pradarśayiṣyanti 
sarveṣu jīveṣu karuṇāyā pālitāyā bhikṣuḥ sarvatra nirbādha gantu samartho bhavati
te na pratibandhakatā sṛjanti 
visuddhimagga 
uparyuktānuśīlane bhayamasti
āsaktiḥ asti 
taddvayena hitakaramanuśīlana doṣayukta bhavitumarhati 
tathāpi bhārasāmyavivekaviśvāsaiḥ anuśīlana karttayam 
dhyānaviṣayatvena aparaviṣayasya grahaṇāt prāk anayā rītyā abhyāsakārī karuṇā khalu pālayiṣyati 
sādhāraṇakarmāṅgatena saḥ avaśyamevaivamācaret visuddhimagga 
anuśīlanagatayathāyathaprasagasthāpanāya 
premakaruṇānirbhara dhyāna bhūmirvā mṛttikā vā yatra samādhikarṣaṇa vā antardṛṣṭikarṣaṇa vā kriyate 
samyag jñānalābhāt paramapi evavidha karṣaṇam avyāhata tiṣṭhati 
aguttaranikāya 
 viśuddhimārgāt uparyuktyanucchedaḥ savādeṣu vā ṭīkāsu vā kevala dṛṣṭāntaḥ yatra spaṣṭam ucyate yat karuṇāyāḥ dhyānātmakamanuśīlana sapadi  
sukhena aparajanamanobhāva prabhāvita karoti  
iya śikṣā dhyānamagnatāyā kṛṣṭā karuṇā prati asāmānyā mātrā prakāśayati 
abhyāsakāriṇo'pareṣā sāhāyya kartu śaknuvanti
na kevala śikṣayā
bhikṣāgrahaṇena
dharmīyajīvanagatadṛṣṭāntasthāpanena
api tu karuṇāsamparkitadhyānātmakonnatisādhanena 
sambhavataḥ
idameva sahānubhūtiśīlānandakarṣaṇamityucyate 
kramikavacaneṣu gotamo vyākhyāti yat kaścid bhikṣuḥ sarpeṇa dāruṇa daṣṭo'bhavat
yataḥ sa karuṇārdracittena sarpāṇā kulacatuṣṭhayena saha sambandha na sthāpayāmāsa 
aguttaranikāya  
 gotama āha  bhikṣuṇā karuṇārdracittena sarpāṇā kulacatuṣṭayena saha samparke sthāpite sati sa na daṣṭo'bhaviṣyat 
 eva sarpadaśanāt ātmanā rakṣaṇāya abhyāsakāriṇaḥ sarpāṇā kulacatuṣṭayena saha karuṇāmayacittena samparka sthāpayet evameva cintayitvā  
 karuṇā me'sti virupakkānā kṛte karuṇā me ca erāpatānā kṛte karuṇā me'sti chavyaputtānā tathā kaṇhāgotamakānā kṛte  
karuṇā me'sti padaśūnyānā kṛte 
tathā ca padadvayayuktānā kṛte 
karuṇa me'sti padacatuṣṭayayuktānā kṛte 
bahupadānā kṛte'pi ca 
padaśūnyā na māmapakurvantu
na ca padadvayayuktaḥ 
catuṣpadāḥ na māmapakurvantu
na ca bahupadāḥ 
sarve sacetanā jīvāḥ
sare prāṇavantaḥ jīvāḥ sare ekatra pavitrāṇi dṛśyāni paśyantu 
kamapi na pāpamāgacchatu 
buddhaḥ aparimeyaḥ
dharmaḥ aparimeyaḥ
saghaḥ aparimeyaḥ 
kintu sarpā
vṛścikā jalaukasa
ūrṇanābhāḥ kṛkalāsā mūṣikāśca sarve parimeyā ea 
mayā rakṣaṇa vistṛtam
mayā rakṣaṇa sthāpitam 
sarve jīvāḥ palāyana kurvantu 
aha bhāgyabhavantamadvitīya staumi 
aha saptasamyagjñāninaḥ staumi 
aguttaranikāya 
yadā gotama āha buddhādayaḥ aparimeyāḥ iti
tadā tasyāśayaḥ  sa buddhasya
dharmasya
saghasya ca guṇān nirdiśati 
aguttaranikāyaṭīkā 
sarpādīnā parimeyo guṇo'sti 
aguttaranikāyaṭīkā 
gotamo bhikṣūṇ pradarśayati yat karuṇāpālana dharmīyasatyavyākhyāna ceti hitakarakarmadvayena te ātmānaḥ rakṣitu śaknuvanti 
hānihīnatā ca parihṛtya hānikarajīvebhyo dūra gatvā tiṣṭhanti 
kiñca sagotrīyavacaneṣu gotamo bhikṣūn upadiśati yat te karuṇayātmanaḥ rakṣitu śaknuvanti 
atra mallavīrasya ca tasya śikṣārthinaḥ ca dṛṣṭānto'sti 
ātmarakṣāviṣaye tau bhinnamata poṣayataḥ 
mallavīra āha aha tvā lakṣyayāmi tva ca mām 
evamanyonyalakṣaṇena paraspararakṣaṇa sambhavati 
āvayoḥ mallakrīḍāpi nirvighna samāpti gamiṣyatīti 
anyataśca śikṣārthī āha  ahamātmāna lakṣayāmi bhavānapi ātmāna lakṣayatu iti 
gotamo vyākhyāti yat kartā śikṣārthinaḥ paddhati saphalamanusaret 
tathā ca upasaharati yat sa kartā manasvitāsthāpanena sadṛśī rītimanukuryāt 
śabdāntaraiḥ ucyate
bhikṣavaḥ sveṣā manasvitāyāḥ unnataye parasparasahayogitā kuryuḥ yā
paryāyeṇa apareṣāmupakāra parokṣataḥ sādhayiṣyati 
bhikṣavaḥ teṣā praśāntaiḥ manoyogaiḥ ca vyahavāraiḥ dharmīyajīvanasamparkitapuraskārāṇāmudāharaṇāni pradarśayiṣyanti 
tathā ca anyebhyaḥ anupreraṇā dāsyanti 
buddha āha  bhikṣavaḥ
ya ātmāna rakṣati sa parānapi rakṣati 
yo vā parān rakṣati sa ātmānamapi rakṣati 
bhikṣavaḥ kathamātmarakṣākārī aparān rakṣati 
punaḥ punaḥ dhyānadhāraṇena
dhānakarṣaṇena
dhyānābhyāsena ca 
bhīkṣavaḥ evamātmarakṣākārī aparān rakṣati
bhikṣavaḥ pararakṣākārī kathamātmāna rakṣati 
dhīratayā hānihīnagayā
karuṇāvasthayā
snehamayayatnāvasthayā ca 
bhikṣavaḥ eva pararakṣākārī ātmāna rakṣati 
yadi abhyāsakārī ātmānamadhikṛtya athavā parānadhikṛtya svīyacittasya yatna gṛṇhāti
tarhi ātmānastathā pareṣāmapi upakāro bhavati 
ṭīkā spaṣṭa vadati  pālayitvā
dhyānavastu cintayitvā
bhikṣavaḥ evamātmarakṣākārī parān rakṣati 
yo bhikṣuḥ pārthivaviṣayagatamānanda parihāya pradhānadhyānavastu aharniśa pālayati karṣati ca so'rhatpuruṣasya daśā labhate 
tataḥ aparo janasta dṛṣṭvā cintayati
'ayamuttamo bhikṣuḥ 
tena yathāriti abhyāsaḥ kṛta iti 
' bhikṣusamparkīyametanmata poṣayitvā sa svargamupāgamiṣyati 
eva 'ya ātmāna rakṣati sa parānapi rakṣatīti 
' 'dhairyeṇa' ityasyārthaḥ dhīratayā sahiṣṇutayā ceti 
'hānihīnatayā' ityasyārthaḥ prāthamikaparyāyagatakaruṇayā saha anukampayā iti 
'premāvasthayā' ityasyārthaḥ prāthamikaparyāyagatapremṇā saha prītyeti 
'sasnehayatnāvasthayā' ityāsyārthaḥ prāthamikaparyāyagatasahānubhūtānandena saha snehānvitasevayā sahānubhūtasukhena ceti 
yaḥ parān rakṣati sa ātmānamapi rakṣati 
asmin prasage
bhikṣuḥ karuṇā
prema
sahānubhūtānandaḥ iti udāttabhāvatrayamadhikṛtya aharniśam ādyaparyāyatrayagatadhyānamagnatāmācarati 
tathā karaṇena sāpekṣavastuvaiśiṣṭya jñātvā arhatpurusasyāvasthā labhate 
eva 'yaḥ parān rakṣati sa ātmānamapi rakṣatīti' 
sayuttanikāyaṭīkā 
arhatpuruṣasḥ pareṣu dharmīyajīvanāt prāpyānā purasārāṇāmādarśabhūtaḥ 
kaścijjanaḥ arhatpuruṣamālokya prītaśca dṛḍhapratyayaśca bhavati 
tathā ca tadīyavyavahāreṇānuprāṇito bhavati 
tasmin samaye hitakarahṛdayavān janaḥ bhaviṣyati kāle arhatpuruṣatvārjanāya kāraṇāni sṛjati 
asya viśvastasya hitakarasya ca cittasya kārānāt sa janaḥ kartṛrūpaḥ maraṇāt para nyūnatamataḥ svarge janiṣyate 
eva yo'bhyāsakārī svīyānuśīlanena ātmāna rakṣati so'rhatpuruṣaḥ san parānapi rakṣati 
yadyapi prema
karuṇā
sahānubhūtānandaḥ ca  iti udāttabhāvatrayānuśīlanena abhyāsakārī aparān hitāvaha ca pratyakṣa ca prabhāvitān karoti
tathāpi savādeṣu anyaviṣayasya ullekho nāsti 
vara yo jana etān bhāvān karṣati
sa tasya citta yathākrama krodhāt
niṣṭhuratvāt paradoṣādoṣāt ca rakṣati iti viṣayeṣu savādā gurutvamāropayanti 
prāgukte savāde gotamaḥ varṇayati yat abhyāsakārī aparān prati tasya manobhāvamadhikṛtya dhīrataya
hānihīnatayā
karuṇāvasthayā
sasnehayatnāvasthayā ca tadīyacitta rakṣati 
karuṇā prema sahānubhūtānandaḥ iti udāttabhāvatrayabodhāya antimabhāvatraya vyākhyāyate 
ayamāśayaḥ  dhyānamagnatāparyāye sārvalaukikapremāditvena te bhāvā gamyante 
aguttaramāśayaḥ  dhyānamagnatāparyāye sārvalaukikapremāditvena te bhāvā gamyante 
aguttaranikāya 
visuddhimagga 
ete udāttā bhāvāḥ krodhādyanaitikavācakabhāvāt abhyāsakāriṇa rakṣanti 
uktabhāvatraya khalu antardṛṣṭermūlatvena vyavahriyate
yathā antardṛṣṭyā abhyāsakārī sarvavidhamānasikadūṣaṇa cira parityaktumagrasaro bhavati 
sa tathākaraṇena sarvavidhānuṣaṅgikaduḥkhaiḥ saha punarjanamana ātmāna muñcati 
tataśca arhatpuruṣaḥ bhavati 
eva parān prati svīyabhāvamavalambya so'bhyāsakārī svīyacitta rakṣati
tenātmanaḥ rakṣaṇa samāpti gacchati 
aya savādaḥ abhyāsakāriṇā dṛṣṭāntamūlakakarmasu tathā dharmīyasamṛddhisamparkitatātparye'dhika gurutvamāropayati 
yadyapi atra sāmājikakarmopadeśānā spaṣṭa ullekho nāsti
 tathāpīda gamyate yat sahānubhūtisamparkitopadeśānā vistṛte pariprekṣite pareṣā kṛte'bhyāsakāriṇā hṛdayānubhūta udvego mukhyataḥ śikṣayā  
karmaniṣṭha prakāśitaḥ  
sāmājikodvegasya ca tadānuṣaṅgikakarmaṇo madhye'nivāryaḥ sambandho'sti  iti vayamanubhavāmaḥ 
pūrvatanasya sarvavidhālocanāparatana yāvadavicchinna vahati 
kintu buddhenātra etāvadanivāryatva nānubhūtam 
sa sahānubhūtiḥ saralākaruṇā
karuṇātmakakarmāṇietatrayasamparkitopadeśeṣu
viśeṣeṇa sahānubhūtimūlakopadeśeṣu sāmājikodvegena saha sāmājikakarmaṇaḥ samparka paśyati 
sa vyaktigatakṣetre tathā sahāyakabhrātrīyakarmaṇi  yatra aparaiḥ saha abhyāsakāriṇo yogo'sti
tat saparkitaparyāyasyopari gurutvamāropayati 
sa premakaruṇāsamparkitadhyānātmakopadeśaiḥ saha paravartiparārthamūlakakarmaṇā sambandha sthāpayitu prayojana nānvabhavat 
yataḥ paravartiviṣayasyopadeśaḥ tenānyatra dattaḥ 
kintu atreda gamyate it īdṛśadhyānānusaraṇāya īdṛśaparārthaparakarmaṇā svābhāvikī pravaṇatā tiṣṭhati 
pālitapremakaruṇālocanākāle gotamaḥ apūrvāṇā guṇānāmupasthāpana karoti
ye guṇāḥ 'sahānubhūtiḥ saralākaruṇāḥ premamayakarmāṇi'  iti eṣā viṣayāṇā prasage prāyeṇa nālocitaḥ 
ete'pūrvā guṇāḥ teṣā rakṣaṇātmakāḥ viṣayāḥ
vyaktigatāstathā manastatvasammatā lābhāḥ
paravartijīvanāya api lābhāḥ 
kramikavacaneṣu gotama upadiśati yat aṣṭau lābhāḥ santi 
kaścijjanaḥ karuṇarūpamanomuktitaḥ tān lābhān arjayitumalam
yadā vā tīvrā
aṅgīkṛtā
vardhitā
pratiśrutitvena pariṇatā bhavati 
aguttaranikāya 
'naraḥ samyak svapiti 
sa samyak jāgartti 
sa suḥsvapnān na paśyati 
sa manuṣyāṇā priyo bhavati 
so'manuṣyāṇā priyo bhavati 
devatāsta rakṣanti 
so'gninā viṣeṇa
astraiśca nābhibhūto bhavati 
tasyopalabdhiryadi mahattarā na bhavati tarhi 'sa brāhmajagat ārohati 
' aguttaranikāya 
ṭīkayā viśleṣaṇamevam  sa bhayaṅkarān svapnān na paśyati 
sa yadyapi paśyati
tathāpi te svapnāḥ kevala śubhāḥ svapnā eva 
sa ātmāna paśyati 
yathā  so'vaśiṣṭādhāre śraddhā nivedayatīva 
athavā buddha
dharma
sagha ca pūjayatīva 
yathā apare janāḥ svapnān paśyanti
tathā sa na paśyati
apare paśyanti  te dasyubhiḥ veṣṭitāḥ
sarpaiḥ tāḍitā athavā vivaramadhye patitā iva 
sa nāgninā viṣeṇāstraiśca abhibhūto bhavati 
asmin prasage kati gokathā kathayanti 
kaścit gauḥ daṇḍāyamānaḥ san vatsāya dugdha dadāti sma 
kaścit vyādhaḥ hastena kunta dhṛtvā acintayat
'aha gāmimam prahariṣyāmi' iti 
tena kunte nikṣipte sati sa kuntaḥ goḥ śarīram āhatya punareva tālapatramiva pratyāgataḥ 
atra praveśaparyāyagatā karuṇā na hetuḥ
na vā sthāpanaparyāyagatā karuṇā api tu
vatsahitāya goḥ sutīvrā ākāṅkṣā 
eva karuṇāyāḥ mahatī śaktirasti 
aguttaranikāyaṭīkā 
karuṇārūpamanomuktisañjātalābhāḥ khalu upari uktāḥ 
kintu ete lābhāḥ svabhāvataḥ sarvāsu avasthāsu ghaṭante iti kadāpi na savādeṣu vā ṭīkāsu vā uktam 
gotamo'pi karuṇāyāḥ sahānubhūteśca mahatī śakti dhṛtvāpi śatruśūnyo nāsīt 
īrṣyāparāyaṇo bhrātā devadatta eva tasya pramāṇam 
vividhāsu daśāsu manaso śaktiḥ ca parārtha tacchakteḥ kāryakāritā cetyanayoḥ madhye samānupātaḥ lakṣaṇīyaḥ 
sahānubhūtiḥ manasaḥ kayācit śaktyā saha viśeṣeṇa nānvitā bhavati 
abhyāsakāriṇaḥ aparānupadiśanti
aparebhyaḥ bhikṣā gṛhṇanti
parārtha ca dharmīyajīvanasya dṛṣṭānta sthāpayanti 
eṣu sarveṣu kṣetreṣu sahānubhūtiḥ paricālikā śaktirityabhidhīyate 
karuṇārdrakarmāṇi karuṇāmayacittasya kāñcit śaktimavalambante 
tāni karmāṇi parahitasahāyakāni
yadyapi karuṇārūpā manomuktiḥ parebhyaḥ kīdṛśa hita sādhayati sa viṣayo nālocitaḥ
tathāpi ida niḥsaśaya gamyate yat karuṇākarṣaṇa kasyāpi sahānubhūti niviḍā karoti 
evañca paravartipararthaparakarmasu prabhāva prakāśayati 
kasyacinmanobhāvasya śaktiḥ
tajjātalābhāḥ
taddoṣapratikārā yadā ekatra niḥsaśaya prakāśyante tadā teṣu madhye pratyakṣayogo dṛśyate 
sahānubhavaḥ prakṛtyā eva grahaṇīyo manobhāvaḥ 
tatra preṣaṇāśaktirasti
tāṛśaḥ sahānubhavaḥ vartamānena vā bhāvinā puraskārena na kadāpi samarthyate 
prāthamikaparyāyagata kāruṇika citta bhikṣujanasya bhikṣābhoga
dhyānābhyāsa bhikṣunāmadhāraṇa ca samarthayitumarhati 
api ca kāruṇikacittapreṣitaparasparasāpekṣakaruṇātmakakarmāṇi saghasya samṛddhaye bhavanti 
tathāpi karuṇārūpamanomuktisañjālalābhāstathā taddoṣapratikārā atīva vicitrāḥ pracurāḥ ca
yata uccaparyāyagatamanaḥsañjātāsāmānyalābhāya eva ātyantiko manoyogo dīyate 
ida niḥsaśayamucyate yat etādṛśa manobalamapi svalpasamāhitabhāvasañjātalābhān janayati 
 uparyukte savāde karuṇājātalābhān ālocya gotamaḥ karuṇāvikāśa praśasyāha aparimeyakaruṇākarṣaṇaśīlasya manasvino purusya nigaḍāḥ kṣaya gacchanti 
sa sasāracakrasya bhittimūla nāśa yātīti paśyati 
yo janaḥ kevala prāṇiviśeṣāya karuṇā poṣayati sa tathākanraṇena hitasampādako jāyate 
yo mahān puruṣaḥ sarveṣā prāṇinā kṛte sahānubhūtiśīlo bhavati sa pracura puṇya sagṛhṇāti 
ṛṣitulyā nṛpāḥ sacetanajīvapūrṇā dharaṇī jayati 
tataśca te katipayayāgakaraṇāya vratī bhavati 
tathā hi  assamedhaḥ
purisamedhaḥ
sammāpasaḥ
vājapeyaḥ niraggalaḥ iti 
 kaścijjanaḥ karuṇāmayacittasya samyakpoṣaṇena yat puṇyamarjayati tasya puṇye yaḥ ṣoḍaśo bhāgastasyāpi ekaṣoḍaśabhāga puṇya te na saccinvanti 
te candramaṇḍale nakṣatrāṇi iva śobhante 
yo na hanti na vā ghātayati aparaiḥ
yo na dasyutā karoti
na vāparaiḥ dasyutā kārayati
sarveṣā bhūtānā kṛte yasyāsti karuṇā sa kamapi jana prati vaira na poṣati 
aguttaranikāya 
nigaḍā kṣaya gacchanti 
sa sasāracakrasya bhittimūla nāśa yātīti pasyati 
ayamāśayaḥ  yo jano'rhatpuruṣasyāvasthā gataḥ sa daśa nigaḍān parityajati 
atra sasāracakrabhittimūlanāśo'ntarbhūtaḥ 
iya daśā yathākrama labhyate antardṛṣṭyā 
asyā asti karuṇā yā ayavahitahetutva vajati 
athavā nigaḍā nāśa yānti 
asyārthaḥ  vidveṣaḥ tathā a vidveṣasamparkitanigaḍā vināśa yānti 
sa sasāracakramiti mūlanāśa paśyati
yataḥ sa karuṇayānvitaḥ san dūṣāṇasvarūpasasāracakrabhittimūlasya tathākathita nāśapaśyati 
aguttaranikāya ṭīkā 
savādeṣu daśavidhā niaḍā sayojana ucyante 
te nigaḍāḥ sasāracakreṇa saha jana badhnanti 
tathā hi  vyaktitvasya mithyā dṛṣṭiḥ
saśayaḥ
yāgādiśāstrānuṣṭhāneṣu āsaktiḥ
indriyākāṅkṣā
krodhaḥ
rūpajagate ākāṅkṣā
rūpahīnajagate ākāṅkṣā
padasthitisacetanatā
mohaḥ avidyā ca 
yataḥ arhatpuruṣeṇa ete nigaḍāḥ apasriyante
tataḥ tena sasāracakrīyasamagrabhittimūlanāśaḥ upadhā kriyate 
anena paunaḥpunikaduḥkhādiyuktapunarnavīkṛtajanmanaḥ kāraṇa nāvaśiṣyate 
vividhāsu ṭīkāsu ālocitānā dūṣaṇānā parityāgāya spaṣṭopāyadvayamullikhati ṭīkā 
tathā hi  antardṛṣṭidvārā dūṣaṇānām unmūlanena sthāyiparityāgasyopāyaḥ samucchedappahāna
 samādhidvārā dūṣaṇānāmavadamanena asthāyiparityāgasyopāyaśca vikkhammanappahāna 
prathama bhāṣyamarhatpuruṣa nirdiśati avyavahitakāraṇatvena aparimeyakaruṇayā saha antardṛṣṭi pālayati 
sakṣepeṇa
sa karuṇāyā upari dhyānena dhyānamagnatāparyāya yāvat samādhi pālayitvā sthāsyati 
 tataśca dhyānamagnadaśyāyā utthāya sa cittasya ca śarīrasya ca viśiṣṭān tathā sāmānyān guṇān praveṣṭu guṇān praveṣṭu tadīya sutīkṣṇa citta  
niyojayati  
 pariṇāme cittasya ca śarīrasya ca pratyeka viṣayamasthāyina parivartanaśīla tathā anirbharayogya paryavekṣya tasya citta svabhāvataḥ tasya  
nirvāṇasyānusandhāna karoti yat sarvavidha pārthiva parivarttana tathā asthāyitvamatikramya vartate  
 parivartanaśīla jagat tathā parivartanahīna nirvāṇamadhikṛtya gabhīrāyāmantardṛṣṭau sañjātāyāmindriyākāṅkṣādimānasikanigaḍaiḥ bandhanasya  
prāvaṇya dūrībhavati  
yāḥ sarvāḥ pratikriyāḥ cira parityaktavyāḥ tāsā na samarthana karotyaya navāviṣkṛtaḥ bodhaḥ 
dvitīyā vyākhyā savāde ullikhita kamapi jana viśliṣyati yasya kevalamaparimeya premāsti 
īdṛśo janaḥ sampūrṇa kintu alpakāla vidveṣamūlakasarvaviṣayebhyo muktastiṣṭhati 
atra 'vidveṣambandhinigaḍāḥ' vidveṣasambandhyāhitakaramānasikadoṣān nirdhiśanti 
tathā hi  asūyā
sañjayaḥ udvegaśca visuddhimagga  
yadā buddha āha
'sa sasāracakrīyadūṣaṇarūpabhittimūlasya tathākathita vināśa paśyati
' tadā sa samāhitapremṇā dūṣaṇānāmasthāyi avadamana nirdiśati 
abhyāsakāriṇo dūṣaṇāni dhyānamagnadaśāyāḥ paramapi dṛṣṭigocaratā gantumarhanti 
tathāpi premadhyānakāle dhyānamagnapuruṣaḥ tadīyadūṣaṇānā samīkṛtāvadamanena saha tṛptikara parama sukhamanubhavati 
 aparimeyapremapoṣaṇāt so'ntardṛṣṭimaktaye bhittimūlatvena īdṛśamānasikāvasthādvārā athavā īdṛśamānasikāvasthāsañjātaparamasukhabhogadvārā upakṛto  
bhavati  
kramikavacaneṣu ekādaśalābhaviṣayake'dhyāye gotamaḥ ekādaśasakhyakānā lābhānāmekā sūcī dadāti 
yo janaḥ premarūpamanomukti sādhayati sa janaḥ tān lābhānarjayati 
prāguktāṣṭalābhaiḥ saha sayojanametat  'sa śīghra tasya citta samāhita karoti 
tasya varṇa ujjvalo bhavati 
sa nirudvegena mriyate' 
aguttaranikāya  
niḥsandehena etat sarvalābhakāraṇāt gotamaḥ punarapi upadiśati yat cāndrāyaṇavrateṣu uposatha
mahatāmācāryāṇā śiṣyāḥ sareṣā bhūtānā kṛte premakaruṇānvitāparimeyahṛdayavikāśāya abhyastā āsan 
aguttaranikāya 
brahmā karuṇāpremasahānubhūtānandasamavṛttitvabhāvān karṣati ca pālayati ca majjhimanikāya 
aguttaranikāyaṭīkā 
tasmāt jīvaddaśāyā prāguktabhāvānā karṣaṇameva brahmasāyujyārjaāya rītiviśeṣaḥ 
gotama imā rīti varṇayati  vāseṭṭha
kaścit bhikṣuḥ karuṇāsahānubhūtānandasamavṛttitānvitacittena satatamekasyā diśi sattāvadbhiḥ bhūtaiḥ saha sambandhitaḥ tiṣṭhati 
tathā ca dvitīyasyā tṛtīyasyā caturthyā ca diśi
upari
adhaḥ pārśvāpārśvi ca tādṛśamācarati 
sa sarvatra viśvabhūtaiḥ saha sambandha sthāpayati samabhāvena  premamayacetasā
yatra cetaḥ tiṣṭhati nirākula
vairānmukta
viśāla vistṛta tathā aparimeyam 
vāseṭṭha ekaḥ śaktiśāliśaṅkhavādakaḥ svalpaceṣṭayā catasṛṣu dikṣu pratidhvani sraṣṭu śaknoti sma 
tatra parimeya karma na parimeya tiṣṭhati 
karuṇāsahānubhūtānandasamavṛttitānvitamanomuktisādhanena tādṛśī avasthā jāyate 
vāseṭṭha ayameva brahmasāyujyamārgaḥ 
dīghanikāya 
punaśca eko bhikṣuḥ ekasyā diśi yathā uttarasyām
sattāvadbhiḥ bhūtaiḥ saha satata samparka sthāpayati premamayacetasā 
tadvat dvitīyasyā tṛtīyasyā caturthyā ca diśi
upari
adhaḥ
pārśvāpārśvi ca samparka sthāpayati 
sa samabhāena sarvatraviśvabhūtaiḥ saha sambandhitastiṣṭhati  premamayacetasā  yatra cetaḥ nirākula
varānmukta
viśāla
vistṛta tathā aparimeyam 
vāseṭṭha ekaḥ śaktiśālī śaṅkhavādakaḥ kevala svalpaceṣṭayā catasṛṣu dikṣu pratidhvani sraṣṭu śaknoti sma 
tatra parimeya karma na parimeya tiṣṭhati 
premamayamanomuktisādhanena sadṛśī avasthā jāyate 
vāseṭṭha ayameva brahmasāyujyamārgaḥ 
yadā prāguktopadeśānusārataḥ premādayaḥ kṛṣyante tadā te eva udāttā bhāvā ucyante 
aguttaranikāya 
savādeṣu ādyasakalanacatuṣṭāye karuṇāpremasahānubhūtānandasamavṛttitānā lakṣaṇāni na kṛtāni 
tathāpi ṭīkābhiḥ viśuddhimārgeṇa ca teṣā viṣayāṇā lakṣaṇāni tathā vyākhyānāni kṛtāni 
pratyekodāttabhāvasya spaṣṭavaiśiṣṭyāstīti kāraṇāt ekasmin bhāve upasthite apareṣā bhāvānāmanupasthitirgamyate 
paradūhkadūrīkaraṇāya karuṇāyā bhaktirūpa vyaiśiṣṭyamasti 
paraduḥkhakātaratā eva karuṇāyāḥ karma 
visuddhimagga 
karuṇāyāḥ dhyānātmaka karṣaṇa hisāpratirodhāya viśeṣeṇa phalapradam 
visuddhimagga 
sahānubhūtānandasya prītiprada lakṣaṇam asti 
visuddhimagga 
anasūyā eva tasya karma 
visuddhimagga  
sahānubhūtānandasya dhyānātmaka karṣaṇa hi asantoṣapratirodhāya viśeṣataḥ phalapradam 
visuddhimagga 
samavṛttitāyāḥ samamanobhāvāpanna lakṣaṇamasti visuddhimagga 
 yo manobhāvaḥ sacetanajīveṣu tiṣṭhati 
samabhāvena sarvajīvadarśanameva samavṛttitāyāḥ karma 
visuddhimagga 
samavṛttitāyāḥ dhyānātmaka karṣaṇa nāma rāgapratirodhāya viśeṣataḥ phalapradam 
samavṛttitārūpa udātto bhāvaḥ samavṛttitānubhavāt pṛthak 
pūrvatra sacetanajīvaviṣayikī nirapekṣatā varttate 
kintu paratra na sukhasya
na vā duḥkhasyānubhūtiṣṭhiṣṭhati
yā sacetanamanasaḥ vividhāsu daśāsu sahacaro jāyate 
visuddhimagga  
eteṣā caturṇā bhāvānā karma khalu janapreṣaṇamūlakam 
 parama jyotiḥ sāra dadāti  'sarve jīvā etebhyo duḥkhādibhyo muktā bhavantu' evavidhayā cintayā paraduḥkhakaṣṭadūrīkaraṇāya ākāṅkṣādaśā  
hi karuṇā  
'sarve jīvāḥ sukhino bhavantu' evavidhayā cintayā sukhahitasādhanāya ākāṅkṣādaśā hi prema 
'yūyamānandamanubhavatha 
ida sādhu yat yūyamānandamanubhavatha 
idamatīva sādhu'  iti cintayā satata parasukhahitasādhanecchādaśā eva sahānubhūtānandaḥ 
'atītakarmaphalakāraṇādeva janasya sukhāni ca duḥkhāni ca bhavanti' iti cintayā parasukhaduḥkhaviṣayikī abhijñatā eva samavṛttitā 
caritracitraṇeṣu ca sārasagraheṣu ca virodhābhāso dṛśyate 
tathā hi  prema paramaṅgalasādhanāya bhaktitvena lakṣyate 
prema hi sukhasādhanecchādaśā 
atra karmapratiśrutirgramyate 
tathāpi 'sarve sukhino bhavantu' itīcchāyā premṇaḥ sārarūpa vartate  yatra karmapratiśrutibhāvanayā prayojana nyūnameva dṛśyate 
sambhavato'tra heturhi eva bhavitumarhati 
yathā  savādeṣu ullikhitāḥ premakaruṇāviṣayakopadeśāḥ kevala dhyānayogena eteṣā bhāvānāmanuśīlana nirdiśanti 
ata eva upadeśāḥ kevala 'sarve sukhino bhavantu' 'sarve duḥkhānmuktā bhavantu' evavidhecchānuśīlanamāvahati 
premakaruṇādhyāna ca pareṣā kṛte ānuṣaṅgika karma cāntarā ko'pi sambandhaḥ gotamena kadāpi noccāritaḥ 
tathāpi ida gamyate yat eteṣā bhāvānā karṣaṇena dhyānino janasya bhrātrīyakarmaṇā prakṛtau tathā paridhau parivarttana sūcyate 
yo'bhyāsakārī samāhitasārvalaukikapremakaruṇānuśīlana karoti
so'vaśyameva janahitasādhanāya gabhīra vicalito bhaviṣyatītyatra na ko'pi vyaktikramaḥ 
premamayakarmaṇā ca saralāyāḥ karuṇāśca sahānubhūteścopari ye upadeśāḥ santi
teṣu premakaruṇayoḥ karmamayī dik varṇitā 
eteṣāmupadeśānā bindumātra vastu api
na dhyānamūlake prasaṅge sīmitam 
eṣu upadeśeṣu gotamaḥ sāmājikakarmapreṣaṇāmupadiśati iti gamyate 
tatra premakaruṇāsavādeṣu dharmīyajīvanasya adhikacintāmūlakabhāvasya gurutva na laghu āsīt 
tathāpi gautamena tannollikhitam  yadi duḥkha jāyate tarhi karuṇā mithyā bhavati 
visuddhimagga 
yadyapi kevala duḥkhaprakāśena karuṇātmakatā prakāśyate
tathāpi karuṇāyā tādṛśī avasthā nāsti 
'sarve duḥkhānmuktā bhavantu' kevalamevavidhā icchā karuṇāyā tiṣṭhati 
paraduḥkhenābhibhūtāḥ santaḥ vaya parān sāhāyya na kurmmaḥ 
ekataḥ hṛdayahīnatā anyataśca paraduḥkhena vihvalatā anayormadhye duḥkhamantareṇa yatnasya vikalpo vartate 
karuṇākarṣaṇakāle jātaduḥkhadūrīkaraṇāya abhyāsakārī satata sacetanaḥ syāt 
sa prathamataḥ atiduḥkhārtajanamadhikṛtya icchati 'sa duḥkhamukto bhavatu' iti 
tataḥ sa priyajanāya
nirapekṣajanāya śatrusthānīyajanāya ca karuṇā karṣati visuddhimagga  
yadi śatrujanaviṣayamadhikṛtya praśno jāyate tarhi prāyukta pratiṣedhaka prayujyate 
karuṇā yathā udāttabhāvarūpā bhavati tathā karaṇāya abhyāsakārī karuṇā samīkuryāt
dṛḍhīkuryāt sāmānyīkuryācca 
idamullekhārha tat pālisavādeṣu ṭīkāsu ca premaśabdo yamartha sūcayati
āgalabhāṣāyā premaśabasyārthaḥ tasmāt pṛthak 
savādeṣu prema na dāmpatyapremāthavā laiṅkikaprema 
kasmiścit gurutvapūrṇe savāde gotamaḥ yathāyatha dāmpatyasamparka vyākhyāti yat svāmī tadīyā striya seveta
strī api tataḥ para ta prati sahānubhūtiśīlā bhavet 
udāttabhāvarūpapremakarṣaṇāya viparīta liṅga prati premṇaḥ prakāśo na karttavya ityupadeśaḥ navadīkṣitebhyo dīyate
yataḥ tathā kṛte prema sukhena tṛṣṇātvena pariṇata bhavati 
visuddhimagga  
abhyāsakārī sarvadā āsaktiparihārāya avahitaḥ syāt anyathā premavikāśo yathāyatha na bhavati 
visuddhimagga 
yatna kṛte ida sambhavati 
dhyātā prathamataḥ ātmāna prati kramaśaḥ premakarṣaṇena premaparidhi vistṛta karoti
tataḥ śraddheyamācārya prati
mitra prati
nirapekṣajana prati pariśeṣe ca śatrujana prati 
tasya lakṣya bhavet samāhitasārvalaukikaprema 
tataḥ so'vaśyameva ida samīkuryāt
dṛḍhīkuryāt tathā vistṛtīkuryāt 
tatra sārvalaukika prema ātmaparabheda na karoti 
visuddhimagga 
sahānubhūtānandasyārthaḥ pareṣā sāphalye prītimayatā 
yadātra parihāsaḥ mattatā vā vartate 
ko'pi vā yadā parasāphalyena ātmavismṛto bhavati tadā sahābubhūtānando bhithyā jāyate 
visuddhimagga 
yathāsambhava hitakaramanaḥpakṣe suṣamatayā prayojanamasti 
parasāphalye'tisasattivaśataḥ suṣamatāyā hānirjāyate 
sā hāniḥ ahitāya bhavati 
eva viśuddhābhyāsāt vicyutirbhaviṣyati 
sahānubhūtānandakarṣaṇāya priyamitrasya gatamāgatamanāgata vā sāphalyamadhikṛtya ānandakarṣaṇamārabhate 
viśuddhimagga 
tataḥ sa yathākrama nirapekṣajanasya ca śatrujanasya ca sāphalyamadhikṛtya sahānubhūtānanda karṣati 
eva premakaruṇākṣetre yat kriyate tadapi ānuṣaṅgikaparyāyeṣu sa karoti 
samavṛttitā parasukhaduḥkhadarśanena sampūrṇasuṣamacittatā 
kevala dhyānamagnatāyāḥ caturthe paryāye samavṛttitāyāḥ karṣaṇa bhavati 
visuddhimagga 
dhyātāraḥ samavṛttitākarṣaṇāyānupreṣitā bhavanti
yataḥ te ādyodāttabhāvatraye kiñcinmanda phala paśyanti 
teṣu udātteṣu bhāveṣu pratyekabhāvaḥ dhyānamagnatāyā ādyeṣu triṣu paryāyeṣu anyatame paryāye kṛṣyate 
visuddhimagga 
'sarve janāḥ sukhino bhavantu' evavidhecchāpoṣaṇena sacetanajīvakṛtāmodeṣu udvegastiṣṭhati 
ādyodāttabhāvatraya tādṛśena udvegena anvito bhavati 
viśuddhimagga 
kintu samavṛttitā tādṛśenodvegena muktā 
kiñca ādyodāttabhāvatraye anumodanasya vā vidveṣasya vā vyāpārastiṣṭhati 
visuddhimagga 
premṇaḥ rakṣāvaśyameva karaṇīyā anyathā prema āsaktyā vipariṇamyate 
karuṇāpi yathāyatha rakṣitavyā anyathā karuṇā pareṣāmavasthāsu vidveṣeṇa vā duḥkhabhāvena vā vipariṇamyate 
eva sahānubhūtānandaḥ mattatājanako bhavitumarhati 
samavṛttitayā saha tulanāyā kṛtāyā mandaphalatvena uktavipattayo dṛśante
tathāpi samavṛttitāyāḥ evavidhena upāyena rakṣayā prayojana nāsti 
avaśeṣe ādyodāttabhāvatraya sukhānubhavena sahānvitam
yataste bhāvā vairāt
hisāyāḥ asantoṣāt ca mukterupāyā eva 
te sarve punaśca duḥkhena api yuktāḥ 
visuddhimagga  
 dhyānamagnatāyāścaturthe paryāye samavṛttitārūpodāttabhāvena saha yaḥ samavṛttitānubhavastena saha tulanāyā kṛtāyā dhyānamagnatāyāḥ ādyaparyāyatrayasañjāta  
parama sukha sthūlameva dṛśyate  
samavṛttitā mithyā bhavati yadi tatra kevala jñānahīnatā vartete 
visuddhimagga 
samavṛttitāyā yathāyatha kṛṣṭāyā satyā iyamupalabdhirjāyate yat anye janāsteṣā karmaṇā kartāraḥ 
evañca teṣāmuttarakālīnā avasthā varttamānakarmaṇā nītigatā dṛṣṭibhaṅgī prativimbiyiṣyati 
visuddhimagga 
yadā dharmaḥ suphalāya kalpateḥ tathaiva adharmaḥ viparītaphalāya sampadyate 
visuddhimagga 
apare janāḥ pariṇāme sveṣā bhāgyāya bhāra niścitameva grahīṣyanti 
eva ca abhyāsakārī tasya bhāgyāya bhāra grahīṣyati
etadviṣayamadhikṛtyāvahitaḥ san dhyātā puruṣaḥ amaṅgalajanakamano bhāvāt tathā paravyavahāragatavidveṣāt tadīya manaḥ mukta karoti 
tathā ca sa dhyānamagnatāyāḥ caturthe paryāye hitakāriṇī paksapātahīnatā poṣayati 
samavṛttitārūpodāttabhāvakarṣaṇāt prāgeva abhyāsakārī dhyānamagnatāyāḥ tṛtīya paryāya yāvat aparodāttabhāvānāmekatama poṣayet 
viśuddhimagga 
sa samāhitadaśāyā utthāya svābhāvikanirapekṣajana ca mitra ca śatru ca adhikṛtya samavṛttitā pālayati 
paravartiparyāyeṣu sa pūrvavadācarati 
yadā so'nena bhāvena dhyānamagnatāyai sāgraha ceṣṭaye tadā avaśyameva caturtha paryāya gacchati 
ayameva kevala vyatikramaḥ 
iayamevodāttabhāvasya prakṛtiḥ 
tā prakṛtimavabudhya vaya śaṅkhavādakasya prāguktāmupamā pratigantu śaknumaḥ 
ṭīkā viśliṣyati  vāseṭṭha
kaścit śaktiśāliśaṅkhavādaka āsīta 
evañca kaścit durbalaḥ śaṅkhavādakaḥ śaṅkhavādanakāle catasṛṣu dikṣu pratidhvani sraṣṭu samartho na bhavati 
sa sarvatra pratidhvanivistārāya nālam 
anyataśca śaktiśālī śaṅkhavādakaḥ sarvatra dhvani vitanitu śaknoti kṛṣṭamanomuktidvārā asmin prasage yā karuṇā 
yadā karuṇāprasaga āyāti
tadā praveśaparyāyagatā karuṇā athavā sthāpanāparyāyagatā karuṇā viṣayopayoginī bhavati 
tathāpi yadā manomuktiprasaga āyāti
tadā kevala sthāpanaparyāyagatā karuṇā viṣayopayoginī bhavati 
yat karma ākāṅkṣāviṣaye vartate tat parimita karmetyucyate 
yat karma rūpayuktaviṣayaka rūpahīnaviṣayaka ca bhavati tat karma aparimeya karmetyucyate 
 parimeyakarmātikramaṇatvāt ida karma aparimeya karmetyucyate viśeṣeṇa sāmānyena ca catasṛṣu dikṣu sambandhavitānatvāt ida karma aparimeya  
karmetyucyate  
tasmin viṣaye na tiṣṭhati
tasmin viṣaye na pratisṭhita bhavati 
ākāṅkṣāviṣayakamadaḥ karma rūpamaye vā rūpahīne vā karmaṇi cira na tiṣṭhati 
ida tatra pratiṣṭhita na bhavati 
ko'syārthaḥ 
ākāṅkṣāviṣayakakarma rūpamaye vā rūpahīne vā karmaṇi āśraya na paśyati 
ātmanaḥ pratiṣṭāyai suyoga na prāpnoti 
kevala rūpamaya vā rūpahīnameva vā karma ākāṅkṣāviṣayakakarma vyāpnoti cātiśete ca 
idamātmanaḥ pratiṣṭhāyai suyoga prānoti 
mahāsamudra ivāya vyāpāraḥ 
mahāsamudraḥ kṣudra jalāśaya parābhūya ātmanaḥ avasara prāpya pratiṣṭhito bhavati 
ida rūpamida vā rūpahīna karma ākāṅkṣāviṣayakakarmaphala pārśve pakṣipati 
idameva brahmasāyujyāya kalpate 
dīghanikāyaṭīkā 
ṭīkā varṇayati yat karuṇā praveśaparyāyagatāmathavāsthāpanaparyāyagatā karuṇā sūcayati 
karuṇā samādhiparyāye dhyānamagnatāyā nimne eva athavā dhyānamagnatāparyāye 
yadyapi iya karuṇā savādeṣu vivṛtāyāḥ karuṇāyāḥ prakṛtena prayogeṇa saha sagacchate
tathāpi manomuktitvena sthāpanaparyāyagatā karuṇaiva gamyate 
tādṛśa viśeṣaṇameva premṇā ca sahānubhūtānandena ca saha prayojyam 
samavṛttitayā sahāpi prayojyam 
samavṛtitā sacetanajīvānadhikṛtya samānamānasikatārthe prayujyate 
 yathā kaścit śaktiśālī śaṅkhavādakaḥ svalpaceṣṭayā catasṛṣu dikṣu pratidhvani sraṣṭumarhati tathaiva kaścidabhyāsakārī manomuktikarṣaṇena catasṛṣu  
dikṣu vartamānaiḥ jīvaiḥ saha sambandhenānvito bhavitumarhati  
yadā śaktiśālī śaṅkhavādakaḥ catasṛṣu dikṣu pratidhvani bhavati 
śabdāntaraiḥ kathyate
na kimapi sthānamasti yatra śabdaḥ na śrūyate 
karuṇādimanomuktikṣetreṣu api tādṛśī avasthā lakṣyate 
kintu asya vyāpārasya ko'rthaḥ 
prathamataḥ
mānasikīmavasthāmadhikṛtya ida sagurutva smartavya yat 'ekṭibhiṭi' iti pada pāliḥ kammala
āgalakarma
cetanā inṭenaśan sūcayati 
visuddhimagga 
'karma' ityasya sthale 'cetanā' ityasya sthāpanena ṭīkāyāḥ sthāna pariṣkṛta jāyate 
durbalena śaṅkhavādakena sṛṣṭa parimeya śabdaplāvanamiva ākāṅkṣāviṣayikī cetanā parimeyā bhavati 
yadā kaścinnaraḥ dhyānamagnatāmarjayati
tadā manaḥ dhyānamagnatāyāḥ ādyaiḥ caturbhiḥ paryāyaiḥ yukte rūpamaye jagati tiṣṭhati
athavā samādhigatamahattārāvasthayā saha yukte sūkṣmatare rūpahīne jagati vartate 
yata udāttabhāvaiḥ saha yuktā mānasikī avasthā dhyānamagnatāyā ādyeṣu caturṣu paryāyeṣu tiṣṭhati
tataḥ sāvasthā rūpamayajagat eva 
rūpamayaviṣayikī yā mānasikī avasthā tayā sahānvitā cetanā rāgādibhāvebhyaḥ sarvathā muktā bhavati
ye rāgādibhāvā manaḥ badhnanti sṛjanti ca parieyatā sīmā vā 
 sā cetanā aparimeyetyucyate 
kiñca udāttabhāvakarṣaṇarato'bhyāsakārī vṛddhiviśeṣeṇāthavā kramaśaḥ pratyeka diśi sattāvad bhūteṣu tān vitanoti
athavā sāmānyena yugapat sarvatra tān vitanoti 
visuddhimagga 
eva caitanyāgataviṣayāṇā pariprekṣite abhyāsakāriṇaḥ cetanā aparimeyā jāyate 
yadā aparimeyā karuṇācetanā vartate
tadā parimeyā ākāṅkṣāviṣayikī cetanā na tiṣṭhati 
 samudrasya ca puṣkariṇyāśca rūpakalpam ullikhya ṭīkā 'yadeva parimeya karma tat tatra prasage na tiṣṭhati' iti vacanasya aparamartha nirdiśati 
yadi kaścit janaḥ tasya jīvanasya kasmiscit samaye udāttabhāvānāmanyatama karṣati
tarhi tasya mṛtyau etadbhāvānvitacetanā sārthakatāmāyāti tathā brāhmaloke tadīyapunarjanmane kalpate 
tasmin samaye kimapi parimeyamākāṅkṣāviṣayagata karma sārthaka na bhavati 
eva brāhmaṇyaloke punarjanmane udāttabhāvānā prabhāvaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ 
 iya vyākhyā dhyānamagnatāyāḥ paryāye karuṇādimanomuktikarṣaṇaphalānāmantarbhāvāya śaktiśāliśaṅkhavādakasya upamāyā vāstavamavasara vitanoti 
savādasyopasahāre gotama āha yat yo naraḥ prāguktopāyena udāttabhāvacatuṣṭaya karṣati
sa strīsasargavairopadravamānasikadūṣaṇebhyaḥ muktaḥ bhaviṣyati 
tathā ca sa manobalamarjayati 
brāhmaguṇasampanno'ya janaḥ maraṇāt para brahmaloka gacchati yadā prema
karuṇā
sahānubhūtānandaḥ
samavṛttitā ca caturvidhānāmupadeśānā rītimanusṛtya kṛṣyante tadā te guṇā udāttā bhāvā iti kathyate 
brahmavihāra
aguttaranikāya 
śabdataḥ udāttā bhāvā hi jīvanayātropāyāḥ vihāra
brahmavat devatāḥ
brahmā
 athavā te bhāvāḥ jīvanayātrāyā utkṛṣṭā upāyāḥ 
visuddhimagga 
pratyekodāttabhāvaḥ krodhahisādyahitakaradoṣaghno'gadaḥ 
eva sarve catvāro bhāvā abhyāsakāriṇe hitāya bhavanti 
 yadyapi nirdiṣṭe samaye kaścit dhyātā eka bhāvamupakāraka matvā tatra gurutvamāropayitum arhati gotamaḥ karuṇābhūtakṛṣṭabhāvasya sārvikeṣu  
lābheṣu gurutvamāropayati 
yataḥ karuṇāsamṛddhakarmāṇi tathā sahānubhūtimadhikṛtya tasya sarve upadeśāḥ karuṇayā saha samparkitāḥ 
karuṇāyā kācid vṛddhiḥ paravarttidvaya sajīvīkaroti arthāt samagradharmīyajīvanasya preṣaṇā ca prakāśanā ca samṛdhyā bhūṣayati 
catvāra udattā bhāvā vā brahmavihārā vā samavṛttitāyā manastattvasammatalābhān pratibimbayanti
yeṣu ādyatraya tulyapadatva bhajati
kintu samavṛttitāyāḥ pada mahattamam 
ekasyā ṭīkāyā teṣā vikāśasya kramaḥ pradarśitaḥ 
pitarau tayoḥ santānānā kṛte yān bhāvān anubhavataḥ taiḥ bhāvaiḥ saha udāttabhāvānā tulanā kriyate 
yadā śiśuḥ garbhasya madhye vartate
tadā karuṇāmayacetasā pitarau 'kadā vā sarvāvayavānvita svāsthyavanta putra drakṣyāvaḥ' iti
tataḥ yadāya komalaḥ śiśuḥ pṛṣṭhadeśe śete
yūkamakṣikādibhiḥ daśanāt athavā nidrāvyāghātakāraṇāt roditi vilapati vā
tadā tat śrutvā pitarau sādharaṇī karuṇāmanubhavataḥ 
 kiñca atīva ākāṅkṣaṇīyavarṣeṣu yadā krīḍākāle śiśuḥ dhāvati athavā viśrāma labhate tadā tadālokya pitroḥ manaḥ śata utkṛṣṭaviśuddhanavanītasiktatūlanirmitakomalakandukā  
iva komala bhavati  
pitroḥ citta paritṛpta cānandita ca bhavati 
tadā tayoḥ sahānubhūta ānando jāyate 
tataḥ yadā putraḥ tasya bhāryāyai bhūṣaṇāni dātu śaknoti tathā ca svakīye gṛhe vasati
tadā pitarau samavṛttisampannau santau arthāt samacittatāmavalamba cintayataḥ 'adhunā āvayoḥ putraḥ svādhinaḥ san sthātumarhati' iti 
eva tau tasmin samaye samavṛttitāmarjayataḥ 
aguttaranikāyaṭīkā 
eva vidhenopāyena
yo'bhyāsakārī udāttān bhāvān karṣati
sa prathamataḥ karuṇā poṣayati 
asmin samaye sa sacetanajīvebhyo hitamicchati 
visuddhimagga 
tataḥ yadā sa paśyati
śṛṇoti
cintayati yat te jīvā duḥkhādhīnāḥ visuddhiagga 
 tadā sa paraduḥkhaūrīkaraṇāya anurāgarūpa prema karṣati 
yataḥ ayamanurāgaḥ dhyānamagnadaśāyā kṛṣyate
abhyāsakārī karmāpekṣayā bhāvavikāśāya samāhito bhavati 
 karuṇākarṣaṇena abhyāsakārī yebhyaḥ hitamaicchat
teṣā duḥkha dūrībhavatu iti aicchat teṣā jīvānā samṛddhi yadābhyāsakārī paśyati disvā
 taā sa ānandito bhavati 
visuddhimagga 
atra 'paśyati' ityasyārthaḥ  dhyātā vartamāne parasamṛdhi samīkṣate athavā atītasamṛddhi bhāvisamṛddhi vā cintayati 
visuddhimagga 
tasya cintā kevala vastugataviṣayeṇa sīmitā tiṣṭhati 
eva sahānubhūtānandakarṣaṇena abhyāsakārī pareṣā kṛte saśliṣṭānā bhāvānā nirmāṇa sapūrayati 
na ko'pi avaśiṣyate 
sa samavṛttitā kraṣṭumarhati
sā samavṛttitā na samānamānasikatāsañjātabhaktiḥ 
sa nirapekṣadarśakaḥ san sarvān jīvān paryavekṣate 
visuddhimagga 
abhyāsakārī vyaktigatalābhāya tathā manastatvasammatalābhāya udāttabhāvānāmekatama pālayitumanu preṣito bhavati 
sa krodhādiviṣaghnāgadatvena prāguktabhāvacatuṣṭaya palayitu pravṛtto bhavati 
upadiṣṭavikāśakramaḥ maulikapratikriyācatuṣṭayādarśamanusarati 
 imamādarśa punaḥ punaḥ anusṛtya abhyāsakārī pareṣā kṛte ghaniṣṭha cintayitu pravartate tasya sāmarthyamapi samānamānasikatayā yukta jāyate 
ida niḥsaśayenocyate yat dhyānena udāttabhāvānā karṣaṇa hitakara
pareṣā prakṛtāsu avasthāsu kṛtā pratikriyā prabhāvitā karoti 
tena prabhāveṇa pratikriyāyāḥ tīvratā
upayuktatā
sthāyitā ca parivartante 
gotamaḥ kadāpi na pratipādayati yat udāttabhāvaviṣayakāḥ caturvidhā upadeśā ekāntata tasyaiva 
yo janaḥ kevalam udāttabhāvānāmanuśīlana karoti sa sādhu na karoti 
 gotamaḥ spaṣṭataḥ muktaye aṣṭāṅgikamārgīyopadesaiḥ saha udāttabhāvānā kevalamanuśīlanasya vaiparītya pradarśayati   caturvidhopadeśānusāreṇa  
karuṇādīnā kevalamanuśīlana parāṅmukhīkaraṇāya 
anāsaktaye
praśāntyai
virāgāya
pratyakṣajñānāya
samyagjñānāya nirvāṇāya ca hitakaratvamāvahati
kintu kevala brahmaloke punarjanme kalpate 
 mamānuśīlana sampūrṇaviṣayavimukhatā sādhayati 
api ca tadanuśīlana viṣayāsaktityāge indriyabhogaviratau
praśāntabhāvalābhe pratyakṣajñānārjane
samyag jñānārjane
nirvāṇalābhe viśeṣataḥ asṭāṅgikamahāmārgāvalambane sahāyakatā vrajati 
 dīghanikāya 
udāttabhāvānā kevalamanuśīlana brahmaloke punarjanmane kalpate 
na tat cita dūṣaṇamukti vā punarjanmamukti kārayitumalam 
brahmādayaḥ api sakaṣṭajarāmṛtyupunarjanmanāmadhīnatā vrajanti 
aguttaranikāya 
 kevala buddhopadiṣṭamārgānusaraṇadvārā nirvāṇalābhāt ko'pi janaḥ pariṇāme nirvāṇaśāntau punarjanma parivartanaduḥkhādibhyo muktimarjayitumalam 
aguttaranikāya 
tathāpi sarve janāḥ kaṣṭanivāraṇāya gotamasya upadeśān grahītumasamarthāḥ santaḥ tebhyaḥ palāyante 
tatrāsamarthā janā anyathā upadiśyante
tatra tu mahattama lakṣya na sādhyate 
ekadā brahmaloke punarjanmagrahaṇāya udāttabhāvānuśīlana kartavyamityupadeśaḥ sāriputtena dhānañjānināmakāya viprāya pradattaḥ 
majjhimanikāya 
tatkṣaṇādeva tathā kṛtvā maraṇāt para sa punaḥ brahmaloke'jāyata 
alokadṛṣṭyā gotama etatsarvamavagatya pratyāgata sāriputtamāha  'sāriputta
apyekadā tvayā utthāya nikṛṣṭabrahmaloke pratiṣṭhito vipro dhānañjāniḥ parityaktaḥ
tasya tu adhikatarasādhanīyavastu āsīt 
' majjhimanikāya  
sāriputto vyākhyāti yat tena sa brāhmaṇo brahmaloke pratiṣṭhāpito yato brahmaloko brāhmaṇebhya eva 
buddhasya praśno nirdiśati yat dharmācāryaḥ śiṣyasya kalyāṇārtha kadāpi paritṛpto bhavitu nārhati 
ācāryo'pi nirdiṣṭe samaye yathāsādhya śiṣya pramodayet 
yataḥ brahmaloke punarjanmagrahaṇamantardṛṣṭilābhānnikṛṣṭataram
śiṣyo yadi paravartisamṛddhaye utsāhī bhavati
tarhi saśliṣṭopadeśadānamācāryasya mukhya karttavyam 
gabhirāntardṛṣṭisampanno jano yadā udāttabhāvān karṣati
tadā prāguktā doṣā na tiṣṭhanti
yataḥ te tataḥ yathāyatha viṣaye kṛṣyante 
 gotamo varṇayati yat sādhāraṇajanakartṛkodāttabhāvakarṣaṇa ca mahata ācāryasya jñāninā śiṣyeṇodāttabhāvānā karṣaṇa cāntarā spaṣṭa pārthakyamasti 
aguttaranikāya 
yadā sādhāraṇo jana udāttabhāvān karṣati
tadā sa maraṇāt para brahmaloke punareva jāyate 
kintu tatratyavāsānte sa punaḥ nārakajanatvena
kṣudhārtapretatvena athavā paśutvena janma grahīṣyati 
aguttaranikāya
  sarvavidhapunarjanmano muktamarhatpuruṣamantareṇa mahata ācāryasya udāttabhāvakarṣaṇarataḥ jñānī śiṣyaḥ maraṇāt para brahmaloke punaḥ  
janiṣyate  
kintu nirantarodāttabhāvānuśīlanāt sa tatra arhatpuruṣaḥ bhavati 
tasmin jīvane samāpti gate saḥ ataḥ para punaḥ na jāyate
kintu amaranirvāṇasamudbhūtā nirāpattāmarjayati 
gautamasya karuṇā prema
sahānubhūtānandaḥ
samavṛttitā ca 
samyagjñānalābhāt paramapi gautamaḥ caturvidhānāmupadeśānā paddhatimanusṛtyanirantara sarvavidhodāttabhāvacatuṣṭayasya karṣaṇa cakāra 
aguttaranikāya 
sarvabhāvacatuṣṭayakarṣaṇe buddha āsīt dakṣa iti sarveṣā nikaṭe spaṣṭamāsīt 
kasmiścit savāde gṛhastho jīvakakomārabhacca āha  'bhadra  mayā śrutam brahmā karuṇayā vasatīti 
' brahmā eva bhāgyavān buddhaḥ
 aha spaṣṭataḥ paśyāmi 
yataḥ bhadra  bhāgyavān buddhaḥ
karuṇayā vasati 
majjhimanikāya 
yata ida mata tiṣṭhati yat brahmaparyāyā devāḥ karuṇā
prema
sahānubhūtānanda samavṛttitā ca cakṛṣuḥ
jīvakaḥ gotama brahmā iti pratipādayati
yataḥ sa paśyati yat gotamaḥ karuṇayā vasati 
gotamaḥ prativadati
'jīvaka
lālasāghṛṇāmohadoṣaiḥ sa 'sadaikyavān' kupito bhavati 
tadartha te doṣāḥ parityaktāḥ
mūlāt vicchinnāḥ
mūlavihīnāstālatarusamāḥ vinaṣṭāśca
te bhaviṣyati kāle udetu na samarthā bhaviṣyanti 
jīvaka etadviṣayamadhikṛtya yat tvayā ucyate
tat mayā gṛhyate iti 
majjhimanikāya 
tataḥ jīvakaśca gotamaśca prema
sahānubhūtānanda samavṛttitā cādhikṛtya parasparāmālocanā cakratuḥ 
gotamo jīvaka jñāpayati yat lālasāghṛṇābhramadoṣaiḥ yadeva bhavatu vā na bhavatu hisā
atṛptiḥ vidveṣapūrṇatā ca vihesāvanta
arativanta
paṭighavanta
nāśa gatāḥ 
eva buddhaḥ sagaurava jīvaka kathayati yat tasya karuṇādisamudayaḥ lālasāghṛṇābhramatyāgamapekṣya sañjātaḥ 
asmin savāde
gotamaḥ krodhahisā'santoṣavidveṣadoṣān premādīnā viparitā iti sthāpayati 
ṭīkāyā gotamasyoktiriya vyākhyātā  jīvaka
eta viṣayamadhikṛtya yat tvayā ucyate tat yadi bhavati  jīvaka
mahān brahmāḥ avadamanātmakatyāgena krodhādīn tyajati 
sa tathā karunayā vasati 
aha nirākaraṇātmakatyāgena tān doṣān tyajāmi 
eta viṣayamadhikṛtya yat tvayā ucyate tat yadi bhavati 
tasyārthaḥ 'yadi ida prāguktiva bhavati tarhi aha te ukti gṛhṇāmi' 
jīvakeneda mata gṛhītam 
tataḥ bhāgyavān buddhaḥ avaśiṣṭodāttabhāvānadhikṛtya tasmai prāguktā śikṣā vistareṇa dadau 
majjhimanikāṭīkā 
brahmā karuṇādīnāmantarāyān avadamanena parityajati 
samyagjñānalābhasamaye tu gotamena sarve mānasikā doṣā unmūlitāḥ 
eva karuṇādīnā karṣaṇasya samaye doṣāvadamanena prayojana nāsāditi kāraṇāt taddamanaceṣṭā tena na kṛtā 
antardṛṣṭikarṣaṇadvārā te sarve kārtsynyena nirākṛtāḥ 
antardriṣṭivikāśāya kaścit janaḥ prathamataḥ viśuddha vyavaharati
samādhi cāvalambate 
viśuddho vyavahāraḥ sarvadā prayojanīyamūlatva brajati
yena so'sadācaraṇodbhūtānutāpāt mukto bhavitumarhati 
visuddhimagga 
viśuddho vyavahāraḥ vartamāne kāle hitakaramānasikatva poṣayati
bhaviṣyati kāle'pi hitāramānasikatva sṛjati 
visuddhimagga 
 hitakaratvasamparkitasādhāraṇasasthānasya madhye eva avasthitaḥ san ko'pi janaḥ samāhitacittasya susaskṛtā avasthāḥ sthāpayitumāśānvito bhavitumarhati 
samādhiyogyeṣu catvāriśatsakhyakeṣu viṣayeṣu visuddhiagga 
 dhyānī jana ācāryopadeśamanusṛtya eka vā ekādhika vā icchati 
visuddhimagga 
tataḥ dhyānī puruṣaḥ manaḥdravyayoḥ sūkṣmaprakṛti praveṣṭhu yantratvena samādhiśāṇita manaḥ vyavaharati 
so'ntardaṣṭi karṣati 
antardṛṣṭimān abhyāsakārī yadi udāttabhāvānā samāhitāvasthāḥ karṣati
tarhi saḥ abhyāsasya spaṣṭaviṣayatvena ubhayasmin viṣaye dakṣo bhavati 
tathāpi ubhaya viṣayamekatrīkṛtya sayuktābhyāsarūpeṇa sa kraṣṭu śaknoti 
'atthakanagarīsavāde' sasārī dasamaḥ ānanda pṛcchati buddhopadiṣṭaḥ ekamātraḥ abhyāso'sti na veti yo'bhyāsaḥ manomukti sādhayati
hānikara prabhāva vinaṣṭa karoti
bandhanāt ca anatikramaṇīyā mukti prasūte 
majjhimanikāya 
ānandaḥ ekādaśābhyāsān lakṣyasādhakān ullikhya uttara dadāti 
tatra ekatama hyevam   kaścit bhikṣuḥ satata premamayacittena ekasyā diśi avasthitaiḥ bhūtaiḥ saha samparka sthāpayati
evañca
dvittīyasyā diśi avasthitaiḥ bhūtaiḥ saha
tṛtīyasyā diśi avasthitaiḥ bhūtaiḥ saha
caturthyā diśi avasthitaiḥ bhūtaiḥ saha 
evañca upari
adhaḥ
pārśvāpārśvi avasthitaiḥ janaiḥ saha sa samparka sthāpayati 
sa samagraviśvasya bhūtaiḥ saha satata sarvatra samabhāvena samparka sthāpayati  karuṇāmayena cetasā

' tasyaivamupalabdhirbhavati

yadi sa tatra karoti
tataḥ sa nimnaparyāyagatanigaḍapañcakanāśa karoti 
tataḥ svargaloke tasya svataḥ sañjāta punarjanma bhavati 
 prāguktā rītimanusṛtya antardṛṣṭi kraṣṭu dhyānī purusaḥ prathamataḥ svābhāvikenopāyena udāttabhāvānāmanyatama karṣati

kintu dhyānamagnatāyā manasaḥ viśuddhatā prakṛtadhyānamagnadaśāyā para kañcit kāla tiṣṭhati 
visuddhimagga 
sa udāttabhāvapoṣaṇa tyajati 
tadā sa vastutattve tathā mānasatatte yādṛśī prakṛtirasti
tasyā anusandhānāya sapadi tīkṣṇa manaḥ niyojayati 
mānasaviṣayāṇā vividhāni kāryāṇi tiṣṭhanti 
tathā ca dehanirmāṇāya vastugatāni upādānāni santi
teṣāmupāānānā kā prakṛtiḥ 
mānasakāryāṇā vā kā prakṛtiḥ 
anayoḥ madhye pārthyakyamanubhavati so'bhyāsakārī
tathā hi  karuṇāyāḥ ko'pi bhāvaḥ bhūteṣu manaḥ sthāpanāya tathā manaḥpoṣaṇāya yuktastiṣṭhati 
tasmin bhāve siddhe ānandamaya utsāho jāyate 
antardṛṣṭimantareṇa
 sthāpana poṣaṇa tathā ānandamayotsāhabhāvaḥ  etāni trīṇi sahavartīni mānasikāni kāryāṇi manasaḥ avibhājyāḥ apṛgbhūtā daśā iva anubhūyante 
antardṛṣṭiyogāt

eva vidhamanusandhāna bahuṣu prasageṣu vividhamānasikakāryeṣu ca punaḥ punaḥ kṛtam 
visuddhimagga 
tadvat akhaṇḍavastunicayah vividhaiḥ upādānaiḥ nirmita iti abhijñatayā pratyakṣīkriyate 
tadā jīvaḥ vāhuḥ
śiraḥ ityādidhāraṇānā sthaleṣu kevala bhautikīmabhijñatā dhyānī janaḥ arjayati 
tatra sa kaṭhināśa komalāśa vā
uṣṇāśa vā śītāśa vā pratyakṣīkaroti

asthāyi asāra ca 
tatra kṣaṇāt kṣaṇāntara dravyagatā calamānatā nāsti 
eva tāni sarvāṇi asantoṣajanakāni 
dhyānī janaḥ pratyaha pratyakṣīkaraṇīyān viṣayān sākṣāt abhijñātu pravartate 
yataḥ abhijñāyamānā cetanāpi vināśaśīlā
tata ida spaṣṭa yat cetanāyāḥ kasmiścit kṣaṇe sampūrṇa vilīne sati aparacetanākṣaṇo jāyate 
visuddhimagga 
 vyaktisattāyā tathā pariveśe parivartanaśīleṣu asāreṣu dravyeṣu śaraṇasvarūpa sthāyinamātmāna nāvalokya dhyānī janaḥ sarvavidhagocaravastu

aguttaranikāya 
eva vastutattvasya navabhāvena pratyakṣīkaraṇāt yogī svabhāvata eva mukti kāmayate 
sa imā mukti nirvāṇasya upalabdhau pratyakṣīkaroti 
tadā sa sarvavidhamasthāyitva ca parivartana cātikramya vartamānāyāḥ kasyāścidavasthāyāḥ sakṣiptaḥ jñāna labhate 
prathame antardṛṣṭigataprāthamikaparyāyeṣu
samāhitacetasā anubhūtāyāḥ asamyaktāyāḥ sutīkṣṇapratyakṣīkaraṇena tasya susthitajagaddṛṣṭiḥ kiyatā parimāṇena viparyastā āsīt 
tataḥ nirvāṇasya upalabdhyā kā eva prakṛtā śāntiḥ iti viṣayamavagacchati 
paramā śaktimanubhūya sa tathaiva atilobhanīyapārthivākarṣaṇaiḥ na punaḥ pralubdhaḥ bhaviṣyati 
ekataḥ sarvastūnāmanirbharayogyatā tathā anityatā yathā spaṣṭā
anyataḥ
tatahiva spaṣṭā nirvāṇasya nirāpattā 
dhyānī janaḥ satata samādhinā tasya cittamavaśyameva śāṇita kuryāt 
gabhīropalabdhisamṛddhaparyāyatrayamatikramya srotaḥpraveśī sannapi dhyānī satatameva antardṛṣṭi pālayet 
eva gocaravastūnāmasantoṣajanakaḥ svabhāvaḥ kramaśaḥ spaṣṭāt spaṣṭatara jāyate 
tadvat nirvāṇasya sāmagrikī viśuddhā prakṛtiḥ satatamadhikatamaspaṣṭatā vrajati 
arhatpuruṣasya phalalābhena antardṛṣṭiḥ sampūrṇā bhavati 
punarjanmanaḥ muktaḥ san maraṇāt para sa nirvāṇasya mṛtyuhīnāmavasthā labhate 
eva vidhenopāyena
bhavacakrāt paramamuktaye bhittimūlatvena udāttabhāvasamūhaḥ vyavahriyate 
srotaḥpraveśinaḥ upalabdhyāpi abhyāsakārī yogī aparān janān antardṛṣṭimārgamupadeṣṭumarhati 
  pañcamo'dhyāyaḥ purāṇā prakṛtistathā prācīnatā ādhunike bhārate saskṛtavidyānuśīlanasyetihāse yadā vaya mudraṇayantrasya vartamāna  
samunnata yuga praviśāmaḥ sma tadā bahuṣu ādyeṣu vastuṣu anyatama vastu prati vibudhānā tathā saskṛtapremiṇā manoyoga ākṛṣṭo'bhavat  
saskṛtasāhityasya mahāgranthānā mudrākanena prayojane eva tat vastu nihita vartate 
saskṛtabhāṣayā viracita mahābhārata bhāratavarṣasya mahattamo granthaḥ samagre viśve'pi asya mahattamattā prasiddhā 
tadgranthaprakāśanāviṣaye eva yugasya udyamasya ca garvaḥ sūcyate 
  tamakhṛṣṭābdāt  khṛṣṭābda yāvat samaye kalikātāsthaiśiyāṭiksosāiṭināmadheyasya pratiṣṭhānasya prasādāt paṇḍitaiḥ saskṛtamahābhārata  
prakāśitam  
asmāt prāk syārauiliyāma jonsmahodayena ātmanastathā pāścātyadeśasya kṛte saskṛtamāviṣkṛtam 
tena kālidāsakṛtasya ṛtusahārākhyasya kṣudrakāvyasya eka saskṛtamāviṣkṛtam 
tena kālidāsakṛtasya ṛtusahārākhyasya kṣudrakāvyasya eka saskaraṇa prakāśitam 
tadṛtusahāra varṇanāmūlaka gītikāvyam 
tatra prācīnabhāratīyaitihyānusāreṇa vastūnā varṇanā vartate 
 tame khṛṣṭābde vagīyākṣarayuktamṛtusahāra tena kalikātātaḥ prakāśitam 
kintu mahābhāratasya prathamasaskaraṇāt para bhārate tathā videśe vibudhamaṇḍalasyābhiniveśaḥ saskṛtavidyānuśīlane kendrībhūto babhūva 
mahābhāratasya prathama saskaraṇa vicāramūlaka nāsīt 
ida sāralyena kati pāṇḍulipīḥ anusṛtavat
yāḥ sampādakaiḥ hastagatāḥ 
idameka sundara saskaraṇam 
ida bahubhirdarśakaiḥ asya abhiprāya pūrṇamakarot kintu anena yathārtha svanaḥ sūcitaḥ 
tataḥ asmābhiḥ jārmānasaskṛtapāṇḍityasūcaka viśāla tathā pradhāna sāhityakarma prāptam 
 yadā ilyāṇḍavāstavyo jārmānadeśīyaḥ paṇḍitaḥ myāksamūlāramahodayaḥ prathamameva ṣaḍbhiḥ khaṇḍaiḥ vibhakta sāyaṇabhāṣyasametamṛgveda sampādya  
prakāśitavān  yo granthaḥ bhārate tathā indoiuropīyajagati prācīnatamaḥ   
ida vicārasambalita prathama mudrita saskaraṇam 
 na kevala taddhastagatapāṇḍulipīnāmapitu anekajīvitapāṇḍulipīnāmarthād yaiḥbhāratīyapaṇḍitaiḥ akhilaḥ vedaḥ kaṇṭhasthīkṛtaḥ teṣā sāhāyyena  
myāksmūlāramahābhāgaḥ vedasya viśuddha pāṭha pratiṣṭhāpayitu yatate sma  
te paṇḍitāḥ pāṇḍulipīnā sāhāyyena pāṭhasya saśodhanāya myāksmūlāra sevante sma 
tataḥ para
vastutaḥ bhārate tathā videśe paṇḍitaiḥ saskṛtaprakāśanasya gauravamaya itihāsa ārabdhaḥ 
kalikātāvāstavyo hemacandravidyāratnamahāśayaḥ vagīyapāṇḍulipimūlasya rāmāyaṇasyaika saskaraṇa prakaṭīkṛtavān 
 gasapāregoresionāmadheyaḥ iṭālīyapaṇḍitaḥ pyārīnagarītaḥ iṭālīyānuvādasametasya rāmāyaṇasyaika prathama vicārasambalita saskaraṇa vyaktīcakāra 
 ttamakhṛṣṭhābdāt  tamakhṛṣṭābda yāvat tasya kālaḥ 
bhārate tathā bhāratād vahiḥ
utkṛṣṭhapāṭhalābhāya paṇḍitaiḥ prabhūto yatnaḥ kṛtaḥ 
tadartha ca kati prakāśanālayā api pratiṣṭhitāḥ tadyathā kalikātāyā jīvānandavidyāsāgarapratiṣṭhitaprakāśanāsasthānam
vārāṇasyā haridāsaguptakṛtā caukhambā saskṛtamālā
bombāinagaryā tukārāmajavajīcālitaḥ nirṇayasāgaramudraṇālayaḥ
punāsthamānandāśramamudraṇagṛham
śrīragam ityasya vāṇīvilāsasamudraṇasasthānam
tathā ca samagra bhārata vyāpya bahavo vikhyātāḥ prakāśanālayāḥ 
tataḥ eśiyāṭikasosāiṭiḥ anyāni pratiṣṭhānāni cāpi etādṛśa karma jagṛhuḥ 
tathā hi  eśiyāṭikasosāiṭidvārā vivliyothekāiṇḍikāsirijaḥ tena saha saskṛtaprakāśanā
trivāndramasaskṛtasirijaḥ
mādrājasya eḍāra thiyojaphīkyāla sosāiṭiḥ
vāgaloraviśvavidyālayasya prakāśanāvibhāgaḥ
prāyeṇa bhārata vyāpya viśvavidyālayalagnāḥ sasthāḥ athavā anusandhānarupaśodhakārya viduṣā samājāḥ yatra kriyate
tathā ca
saskṛtagranthaprakāśanālayāḥ 
etāni sasthānāni saskṛtasampadaḥ pracārāya sayuktāni 
saskṛtasāhityasya viśālatā vismaya sūcayati 
asya sāhityasya anyatama lakṣaṇīya vaiśiṣṭya nihitamasti purāṇeṣu upapurāṇeṣu ca 
mahābhāratād rāmāyaṇāt ca para teṣāmāgamanamabhavat 
  tame khṛṣṭābde punāsthā bhāṇḍārakaraprācyāvidyāgaveṣaṇāsasthā tatrabhavataḥ rāmakṛṣṇagopālabhāṇḍārakaramahāśayasya anupreraṇayā mahābhāratasya  
vicārasameta saskaraṇa prakāśayitumudyoga lebhe  
saskṛte ida karma mahadapūrva tathā ca bhārate prathameva 
vartamāna bhāratasya mukhyeṣu saskṛtapaṇḍiteṣu anyatamasya bhi esa sukṭhaṅkaramahodayasya haste asya karmaṇaḥ bhāraḥ samarpitaḥ 
sa purātanapāṭhasampādanārtha kati niyamān sasarja ye niyamāḥ sarvatra vibudhajagatā susthatvena śuddhatvena ca gṛhītāḥ 
 tasyodyoge upadeśe ca punāyāḥ bhāṇḍārakaraprācyavidyāgaveṣaṇakendrataḥ avaśeṣe mahābhāratasya apūrva viśleṣita saskaraṇa prakaṭībhūtam 
 ida bhāratīyavaidūṣyasyāpūrva nidarśanam  yatra ādhunikapaddhatyā sāhityavicāreṇa saha prācīnasaskṛtavidyāyāḥ ca pāṭhasampādanāyāḥ ca samanvayaḥ  
sādhitaḥ  
samagre bhārate ye hastalekhā āsan
ye ca bhāratād vahiḥ āsan  te sarve sagṛhītāḥ 
bhāratavahirbhūtaśyāmajābhādideśeṣu mahābhāratasya pāṭhāntaratvena ānuṣagika yat sāhitya prāpta tadapi prārthanādhīna kṛtam 
phalataḥ mahābhāratasya mahāsaskaraṇam mahādarśatvena gṛhītamabhavat 
aparaiḥ viśvavidyālayaiḥ sasthānaiḥ ca ayamādarśo gṛhītaḥ 
 rāmāyaṇasyānyāni saskaraṇāni antareṇāpi vālmīkīyarāmāyaṇasya vicārasambalita saskaraṇa mahābhāratapaktitaḥ barodāprācyavidyāgaveṣaṇāsasthānena  
gṛhītam  
āmedāvādastho gujarāṭaviśvavidyālayaḥ bhāgavatapurāasya kārya gṛhṇāti sma 
bhāratīyasaskṛtimukha khalu purāṇam 
bhārata jijñāsuḥ janaḥ purāṇebhyaḥ prayojanīya sāhāyya vāñchati 
prācīnakālādeva purāṇasammatā sabhyatā tathā saskṛtiḥ
paurāṇiko dharmaḥ
paurāṇika darśanam
paurāṇiko viśvāsaśca bhūmaṇḍalasya sarvāsu dikṣu śraddhayā anumoditāni tathā svīkṛtāni 
ata eva purāṇānāmastitve yat calamānatva tat svaya siddhasatyatvena jātam 
ādhunikabhāratīyasamājo'pi purāṇānā bhittau ātmāna niyantu śaknoti 
vastutaḥ purāṇasamūhaḥ hi bhāratavarṣasya bauddhikapragateḥ nirantaro hetustathā protsāhako viṣayaḥ 
ādhunikamanveṣaṇa yadyapi darśayati yat atyalpasasthākāni vidyamānāni purāṇāni yuktyā prācīnakālīyānīti pratipādayanti
tathāpi purāṇasāhityasya mūla vaidikasahitāracanāyuge eva bhavitumarhati 
purāṇasya prācīnatama ullekhaḥ atharvavedasya mandradvaye lakṣyate 
yatraikatarasya ṛcāmiva samapavitramūlyatvam astīti ucyate 
sāmnā chandasā yajusāmiva purāṇānā samayo nitya samucyate 
anyatarakṣetre itihāsena sahāsyollekhaḥ kṛtaḥ 
vaidikasāhityasya bahuṣu grantheṣu itihāsena saha pṛthak vā ekatra vā purāṇasyollekhaḥ kriyate 
tathā hi  śatapathabrāhmaṇe
