ekāgratā
cittaudāryam
apareṣā yathā hānirna bhavati tādṛśīcchā ca 
jīvanasya ca dharmasya ca kṣetre sadācārā upakaraṇaviśeṣāḥ 
te khalu paura jīvana niyamayanti 
jainadharme bauddhadharme ca ahisāmūlo yo dharmaḥ sa vivecanīyamātrayā hindudharma prabhāvita karoti 
vaidikasāhitye yā cintā pracāra labhate
sā cintaiva purāṇānāmapi 
kintu sā cintā janapriyopāyena ākhyānādimādhyamena pracāritā bhavati 
ākhyānādīnā mūlagatāḥ nītiḥ karuṇaiva 
samakālīnabhāvanopayoginī paurāṇikī kathāmālā janapriyaśubhavārttātvena vikhyāyate 
purāṇairvidhṛtā vibhinnā devatāḥ sādhāraṇajīvanopayogivividhāśākāṅkṣāvidhāyinyaḥ iti kāraṇāt tā priyā devātāḥ sañjātāḥ 
paurāṇika sāhitya vicitradharmādarśaviśvāsānā saṅgamasthalam 
sukhabodhyabhāṣayā likhitvāt paurāṇikī vāṇī sudūrasthānīyajanagaṇakarṇasamūhamapi praviśati 
karuṇātmako mahān guṇaḥ api tatra viśiṣṭa gurutva prāpnoti 
aya viṣayaḥ kathopakathādibhiḥ tiryak prativimbito bhavati
yeṣā mūlatvena kriyā kurvanti prema
bhaktiḥ
dānaśīlacittavṛttiḥ
snehaḥ
kṣamā
prativeśisulabhānubhavaḥ ceti 
sarveṣāmeva kendrabinduḥ eva karuṇā 
prāguktabhāveṣu anyatamenānuprāṇitāḥ santa upāsakāsteṣāmīpsitānā devatānā prasādalābhārthamāhvāna kurvanti 
tādṛśamabhigamana vastugatam 
ida hṛdayasya pelavāśataḥ jāyate 
ida japtā devatāḥprati yujyate yā devatāḥ karuṇārūpamūrtisatyaḥ 
bauddhadarśanasya mate sannyāsinaḥ kṣetre karuṇāyāḥ paridhiḥ avaśyameva vistṛto bhavet 
yadi tasya ko'pi śatrurbhavati tarhi ta pratyapi sannyāsī karuṇāparāyaṇo bhavet 
īdṛśaḥ sannyāsī nirvāṇamārgeṇa gacchan sarvavidhapratibandhakebhyaḥ mukto bhavati 
samādhaye'nuśīlana śatrubhāvānmukti na dadāti 
ida kevala hānihīnatāyāmānandānubhavaḥ tathā sarvasmai prītiriti hitāya śatrutā dūrīkaroti 
gahanadhyānena magnaḥ sannyāsī samavṛttisampanne paryāye'vatiṣṭhate 
manasaḥ evavidhāyā daśāyā na kāpi virodhinī śaktiḥ tamapakartu śaknoti 
ata eva īdṛśyā daśāyā sannyāsinaḥ pakṣe
unnatirodhipāpacintādamanāya mānasikyā śaktyā prayojana na bhavati 
viśuddhadaśāmupagatasya viśuddhacittasya sannyāsinaḥ unmārgagamanasambhāvanā sampūrṇatayā dūra gacchati 
tadā sannyāsī dhyānamagnastiṣṭhatu vā svābhāvikadaśāgatastiṣṭhatu vā iti na ko'pi viṣayaḥ 
etādṛśaḥ sannyāsī sarvadā karuṇāmayaśca premamayaśca tiṣṭhati 
sahanaśīla karuṇātmaka citta pratikūladaśāyā pratikriyā na karoti 
vibhnaśūnyadhyānāya jitendriyāḥ sannyāsinaḥ nyūnatamanamanīyavastubhiḥ santuṣṭā bhaveyuḥ iti gotamasyopadeśaḥ 
 aparisīmapremamayacittānuśīlana teṣa karttavyam sādhvida jñāta yat paurāṇikā ṛṣayaḥ jīvikāvyāpāre vā jīvanayāpanavyāpāre vā atīva namanīyā  
āsan  
te āśramajīvanopayoginyūnatamavastubhiḥ kāla yāpayitu śaknuvanti sma 
teṣā citteṣu dayānubhūtiḥ karuṇānubhūtiḥ vā prācuryeṇāsīt 
aya mahān āvegaḥ purāṇānā sarvatra prativimbitaḥ 
devā upāsakebhyo varān dadati
te vipadāpannān bhaktān rakṣanti
vipadaśca tān muñcanti  iti tathya pramāṇīkaroti yat dayādhārā dānadhārā vā teṣu sarvadā sakriyāsīt 
etadapi ghaṭate yat kadāpi vā vararūpaḥ karuṇānubhavaḥ ayogyeṣu api vastuṣu vistāra yāti 
ṛṣayaḥ api tatphalabhoga kurvanti 
ṛṣaya ādhyātmikaprayatnena mahatī śaktimarjayanti 
janahitāya tacchaktiprayoga prāyeṇa te kurvanti 
te'yācitabhāvenaiva svārthaśūnyā sevā yacchanti janagaṇāya 
ida pramāṇīkaroti yat tapasyā teṣā citta viśuddhīkaroti 
tathākaraṇena ca te kārtsnyena svārthaparatāmuktā jāyante 
svārthaśūnyatva tapasyāyāḥ lakṣyam 
ya eva etallakṣyamupagacchati sa ātmaupamyena apareṣā duḥkha vā sukha vā anubhavati 
purāṇāni khalu etaddhāvānuprāṇitaiḥ purāvṛttaiḥ bāhulyena paripūrṇāni 
brahmapurāṇasya  tame'dhyāye kuvarṣerākhyānamasti 
sa sarveṣā kṣunnivṛttaye varāya prārthanā cakāra 
anena tasya māhātmya prakaṭitam 
śunaḥśephākhyāne varuṇasya gabhīrā karuṇā vayamanubhavāmaḥ 
yajñīyabalirūpasya bālakasya sahāyahīnā daśā varuṇasya manasi sahānubhūti tathā karuṇā jāgarayati sma 
sa ca ta rarakṣa 
mahānubhavatāyā bhāvo'pi nimnaprāṇinā hṛdayeṣu lakṣyate 
varāhapurāṇasya  tame'dhyāye kasmiścidupākhyāne kapotasya pecakasya ca bhāryāyugala sādhāraṇakalyāṇāya iṣṭān devān āhvayati sma 
vāmanapurāṇasya  tame'dhyāye vaśiṣṭhasyātulanīyā tyāgavṛttiḥ varṇitā 
evañca purāṇeṣu bahavo dṛṣṭāntāḥ santi yatra tyāgamahānubhavatākaruṇāsahānubhavādīnā tejomayo bhāvo vidyate 
 bauddhaśāstre yathā likhita tathā dṛśyate yat gautamo navadīkṣitān sannyāsina upadiśati yat sannyāsina utthānavicaraṇopaveśanādisamaye samādhyanuśīlanāya  
dṛḍhasakalpā bhaveyuḥ  
tathā ca te yadi upadeśānanusṛtya karma kurvanti
tarhi dhyānasamaye virodhiśaktayo niṣprabhā bhaviṣyanti 
mumukṣuḥ sannyāsī cittamuktaye karuṇābhyāsa kuryāt 
sannyāsinaḥ pakṣe hṛdaye karuṇābhyāso'tīva phalapradaḥ 
tena abhyāsakārī yasmāt kasmādapi ākramaṇāt avamānād vā rakṣaṇāya śaktimarjayati 
kiñca upāsanālaye sannyāsinaḥ ekatra śānta śātu śaknuvanti 
yataḥ hṛdayeṣu karuṇānuśīlanatvāt teṣā hṛdayāni komalāni bhavanti 
tathā ca ekaḥ aparasya uttamaḥ sahacaraḥ bhavati 
nirvāṇalābhāya premakaruṇādhyāna prathamaḥ paryāyo bhūmikāsvarupaḥ 
tathāpi nirvāṇalābhāt paramapi bhūmikāvasthānatvādeva pramaparimalaḥ pareṣā hitāya avaśiṣṭo vartate 
ādhyātmikapragataye sannyāsinaḥ anyonyasahāyā bhaveyuḥ 
eṣāvasthā parokṣabhāvenāparānupakurvanti 
yaḥ sannyāsī pārthiva sukha jahāti sa eva prakṛtaḥ sannyāsī 
sa svīyakarmaṇāparān prabhāitān karoti 
gautamasya mate abhyāsakārī hṛdayena dhīratāhisākaruṇākomalatābhāvānuśīlanena ātmani hṛdaye sahanaśīlatā poṣayati 
ida guṇatrayasyārthaḥ sārvalaukikaḥ premā 
abhyāsakārī yadā sampūrṇa gūḍhadhyānamagnastiṣṭhati tadā guṇatrayamatīva śaktipūrṇa tathā phalapradam 
asmin paryāye abhyāsakārī sarvavidhaduṣṭakarmacintābhyo mukto bhavati
tadā sa bhavacakrād vicchinno jāyate 
yathārthataḥ asmin paryāye abhyāsakāriṇo manaḥ mukta tiṣṭhati 
aya vyāpāraḥ kiyatāpyaśena yājakīyaḥ
atra abhyāsakārī kevala svārtha ceṣṭate
kintu sahānubhūtau harṣaḥ parasukhasajātajarṣa sūcayati 
uktaprasage parārthaparatā gautamasya upadeśeṣu na sūcyate
tathāpi ida niścita yat gūḍhadhyānamīdṛśaguṇāya sampadyate 
purāṇānā kathāsu īdṛśasvārthahīnasevāsambandhidṛṣṭāntāḥ itastataḥ varttante 
purāṇeṣu svārthaśūnyasevāyā mahatī maryādāsti
sevādharmo hi paramaguṇatvena vivicyate 
purāṇeṣu aya guṇaḥ na kevala sādhūnā citteṣu api tu nimnaprāṇinā hṛdayeṣu vartate 
karttavyabodhena saha ātithyādisevā sarveṣā hindūnā sādhāraṇaguṇatvena vivicyate 
kartavyabodho jāyate dayākaruṇānubhavāt 
aya bodho na svalpasthāyī
kintu hinducaritre'vicchedyo guṇaḥ 
atra hindūnā mūlyabodhaḥ pratiphalito bhavati 
pūrvapuruṣāṇā muktaye bhagīrathasya sahanaśīlatā tathā dhīratā svārthaśūnyasevāyāḥ karttavyabodhasya ca ādarśa sthāpayati 
atra sādhusulabhe dayā ca karuṇā ca vartete 
brahmāṇḍapurāṇasya  tame'dhyāye naitikamūlabodhamavalambya nītikathā dṛśyate 
avarajīvānā hṛdayeṣu api kartavyabodhaḥ karuṇābhāvaśca śanaiḥ śanaiḥ praveśa labhete 
 sā ghaṭanā atīva vismayāvahā ca marmasparśinī ca yadā vaya paśyāmaḥ  yo vyādhaḥ vihagamithuna pāśabaddhamakarot tasyaiva kṣudhāyai puruṣo  
vihagaḥ ātmāhūti dātumudyato'bhavat  
samagravyāpāramavalokya sa niṣādo nirvāk tathā āścaryānvito'bhavat 
asmin paryāye sādhāraṇānāmapi janānāmīdṛśaḥ svabhāvaḥ sādhāraṇa eva 
bauddhaśāstrasya mate cittamuktiḥ katipayaguṇasamūhāya bhavati 
yo bhikṣuḥ sādhuḥ arthāt yasya citta sampūrṇa mukta sa kati guṇānarjayati 
so'śubha svapna na paśyati
sa gāḍhanidrā gacchati 
sa bhayaśūnyo bhavati
na ko'pi naraḥ vā paśuḥ vā tamapakartu śaknoti
devāsta rakṣanti tatra daivānugrahe snehabhāvo vartate
 agnista dagdhu na śaknoti
sa paramopalabdhi vinaiva maraṇāt para brahmapada labhate 
sarvopari sahānubhūtiḥ karuṇā ceti guṇadvaya dūḍhadhyānena saha samparkitam
tathāpi taddvaya dhyānamagnatāyā na phalam 
yasyātmopalabdhiḥ sañjātā sa bhavacakrāt punarjanmmo vā muktaḥ 
asya paryāyasya lābhāya karuṇā hi avyavahito hetuḥ
nirāsaktiśca ānuṣaṅgika
hetutva vrajati 
karuṇā gūḍhadhyānasyāparā mūrttiḥ 
kintu abhyāsakārī yadā tapasyāyā kramaśaḥ unnati sādhayati tadā tasya hṛdaye karuṇābhāvo jāyate 
antime paryāye'rthāt nirvāṇasya paryāye sannyāsī sāmpūrṇyena niṣkāmo bhavati 
jāgatikasya vastusamūhasya kṣaṇikatāyā tathā asāratāyā sa sacetano jāyate 
asmin samaye abhyāsakārī pratikūladṛśyaghaṭanācaritrādiṣu pratikriyā na karoti 
yo janmasūtreṇa asīma prema labhate'thavā yasya premamaya hṛdayamasti sa svalpakālena duṣṭamanobhāva niyantu śaknoti 
tataśca yadi sa yatate
sa kramaśa unnati kartu śaknoti 
cāndrāyaṇavratadineṣu mahātmanaḥ guroḥ śiṣyā manasi sarveṣā jīvānā kṛte premakaruṇāmaya hṛdaya poṣayanti 
muktikarṣaṇāt manaḥ virodhiśaktiprabhāvāt mukta jāyate 
manasa īdṛgdaśāyā manaḥ kartsnyena mālinyamukta tiṣṭhati 
tādṛśe manasi karuṇā
sahānubhūtaḥ
ānandaḥ
samavṛttitā cetyādayaḥ guṇā virājante 
tadā brahmasājuyya sambhavati 
karuṇāyā dhyātmaka karṣaṇa kṣatikarapariveśe pratikriyākaraṇāya viśeṣeṇa phalapradam 
premṇo dhyānātmaka karṣaṇa krodha pratihata kartu viśeṣata upayogi 
samavṛttitāyāḥ dhyātmaka karṣaṇa tṛṣṇāyā viruddhe pratikriyākaraṇāya viśeṣeṇa prayojanatva vrajati 
ete upadeśāḥ sāmājikakalyāṇasādhanāya anupreraṇā dadati 
sādhāraṇā janāḥ vṛkṣaropaṇāya
setunirmāṇāya
kṛpakhananāya gṛhahīnebhya āśrayasya dānāya upadiśyante 
atra karuṇā duḥkhārtatāyāḥ kṛpāyāśca vicchinnā bhavet 
arthāt dhyātā puruṣaḥ kadāpi na paraduḥkheṣu kṛpānubhavenānupreritaḥ bhavet
yena sa paraduḥkha vā parakaṣṭa dūrīkartumagrasaro bhavati 
dhyātuḥ pakṣe karuṇāyā aya bhāvaḥ satata svābhāviko bhavet yainānupreritaḥ san sannyāsī apareṣā duḥkha dūrīkartumāgacchati 
dhyātuḥ svābhāvikī pravṛttiḥ prāyeṇa rakṣayituḥ pravṛttiriva bhavet 
paurāṇikakathākārāṇā sādhūnāmiya svābhāvikī pravṛttirāsīt 
te kadāpi kutrāpi vā svābhāvikapravṛttiviruddha karma nākurvan 
teṣāmāsīt dhyānātmikī tathādhyātmikī śaktiḥ 
tayā te'dbhuta karma kartu samarthā āsan 
tathāpi te tacchakteḥ apaprayoga na cakruḥ 
te janahitāyaiva alaukika karma kṛtavantaḥ 
teṣā komala hṛdaya snehabhāvasya āśrayasthalam 
snehaḥ eva tebhyo janasevāyai preraṇā dadāti 
svecchā tiṣṭhatu vā na tiṣṭhatu vā te karuṇātmakapravṛttivaśāt janahitakara kārya sādhayanti 
muneḥ saubhareḥ ākhyāne snehabhāva sahānubhūtiśca nirdiśyete 
taddvayaprabhāvāt sa svaya sundarataruṇarūpa dhṛtvā pakṣapātahīnavyavahāreṇa sarvāsā bhāryāṇā tṛpti vidhadhāti sma 
skandapurāṇasya kasmiścidākhyāne putrāya kārttikeyāya pārvatyāḥ apūrvamātṛsneho'smābhiḥ dṛśyate 
viṣṇupurāṇe vaya paśyāmo yat kena prakāreṇa bhagavān viṣṇuḥ snehāt garuḍasyācaraṇa svābhāvikamakarot 
bauddhānā mate dhyātuḥ sahānubhūta ānandaḥ
prema
karuṇā ca tadaiva nirdoṣatva vrajanti yadā dhyātā nirvāṇamārgasya caturtha paryāyamaupagacchati 
asmin paryāye samavṛttitā dhyātuḥ pakṣe atīva vāstaviko vyāpāraḥ 
antardṛṣṭikarṣaṇena krodhāt
śatrubhāvāt
asantoṣāt lobhāt ca muktiḥ jāyate 
purāṇamapi ātmopalabdhaye dhyānasyopari gurutva sthāpayati
anyavidhayā praceṣṭayā prayojana na bhavati 
bauddhaśāstre upadeśo dīyate yat ācāryasyopadeśaiḥ dhyātāraḥ teṣāmindriyāṇā śakti vardhayiṣyanti 
tataśca samādhiyogena antardṛṣṭiḥ puṣṭi gacchati 
premasamavṛttitādīnām īpsitavastūnā siddhiḥ asthāyinī 
kintu yadā dhyātā dhyānayogena antardṛṣṭeḥ upari sthāpyate tadā krodhatṛṣṇādivirodhibhāvā svata eva dūra gacchanti 
manmayī upalabdhiḥ śreṣṭhatvasyāsane sthāpitā 
yadyapi bauddhaśāstreṣu navadīkṣitānā kṛte tanmayī praceṣṭā upadiśyate
tathāpi teṣā pakṣe manmayī upalabdhiḥ api upayogitva vrajati 
aya vyāpāraḥ sampūrṇa navadīkṣitasya mānasikī sthiti tathā jīvana prati tasya manobhāvamapekṣate 
kintu sarvadaiva karuṇākarṣaṇamavaśyameva karttavyam 
sattāsu manaḥsthāpane tathā manaḥpoṣaṇe karuṇābhāvasya antarbhuktistiṣṭhati 
asya bhāvasya siddhau ānandamayaḥ rasa āvirbhāvati 
antardṛṣṭi vinā sthāpana poṣaṇa tathā ānandānubhavanamiti sahāvasthitamānasikakarmatraya manasi apṛthaktvena avibhājanīyatvenānubhūyate
antardṛṣṭau satyā mānasikavyāpāratrayamadaḥ pṛthak pṛthak prakāśate
pṛthak pṛthak ca kārya karoti 
sacetanamānasakṣetrasya gatiśīlatayā aya vyāpāraḥ sambhavati 
yadā etattraya dhyānayogena samanvitabhāvena prativimbita bhavati tadā sthirapariveśasya kṣaṇikatā
bhaṅguratā
asthiratā ca upalabhyante 
sarve viṣayāstadā duḥkhamayāḥ kaṣṭamayāḥ svatantrāḥ śūnyamayā iva yoginaḥ nikaṭe pratibhānti 
asmin paryāye svārthaśūnyaḥ san yogī sampūrṇā muktimicchati 
sa tā mukti paśyati nirvāṇadaśāyāmeva 
tannirvāṇa punarjanmaśṛkhalāt dūre tiṣṭhati 
tadā sa sampūrṇakaruṇāyā sthāpito bhavati 
idameva mūla tattva bauddhadarśanasya 
paurāṇikasādhūnā karuṇāsahānubhūtimahattvādayo guṇāḥ āsan 
evavidhā bahavo dṛṣṭāntā asmābhiḥ dṛśyante 
sādhāraṇataḥ
sahānubhavasya mahatī anubhūtiḥ tīvrātmīyatābodhājjāyate 
kintu ṛṣīṇā kṣetreṣu svata eva tādṛśī'pekṣikatā phalavatī na bhavati
yataḥ ṛṣaya ātmāna jānanti
jagataḥ prakṛtā sattā pratyakṣīkarvanti
tathā ca te teṣā pṛthagastitva vismaranti 
phalaśrutau te sarvābhiḥ sattābhiḥ saha ātmamatā svīkṛtya aparānubhūta duḥkha nijavadanubhavanti 
karuṇāsahānubhūtisamparkito'pūrvo dṛṣṭāntaḥ matsyapurāṇe dṛśyate 
tatra kumbhīrākrāntabālaka prati śivabhāryāyā umāyāḥ sahānubhūtiḥ karuṇā ca prativimbite 
rājarṣīṇā bharatenāpi avarajīvān prati karuṇā kṛtā 
vayametadākhyāna viṣṇupurāṇe paśyāmaḥ 
abhiyojanasya bhāvāt kṣamānubhavo jāyate  yā kṣamā aparādhina janamuddiśya kriyate 
purāṇeṣu ṛṣibhiḥ aparādhina prati dayāyāstathā kṣamāyāḥ pradarśanamadhikṛtya vṛttāntā bāhulyena dṛśyante 
purāṇānāmākhyāne vaya paśyāmo yat kaścidṛṣiḥ karuṇāvaśāt uccāritamabhiśāpamapanayati 
kūrmapurāṇe kasmiścidākhyāne vaya paśyāmo yat muninā gautamena uccāritaśāpasambhūtadaṇḍasya hrāsaḥ kṛtaḥ 
eva vaya paśyāmaḥ  vaidikasya tathā paurāṇikasya darśanasya mataiḥ saha bauddhadarśanasya matānā niviḍa sānnidhya vartate 
tat sānnidhyamubhayordarśanayormadhye anyonyātmīyatva sūcayati 
ubhayordarśanayormadhye asmin cāritrike sambandhe sati hindubhiḥ daśāvatāreṣu anyatamāvatāratvena buddhadevaḥ svīkṛtaḥ iti
